./       ADD   NAME=CLONER
/**  REXX -- CREATE ANOTHER VERSION OF A D/S UNDER ISPF 3.4  **/

   PARSE ARG PARMS
   MSG = MSG(OFF)
   PARMS = TRANSLATE(PARMS)

   ZINPDSN = ""
   ZNEWDSN = ""
   OPTION  = ""
   NUMOPT  = ""
   NUMCHG  = ""
   RELOPT  = ""
   Q       = 0

   IF WORD(PARMS,2) = "" | WORD(PARMS,1) = "?"
      THEN SIGNAL DISPDOC

   DO II = 1 TO 9
      TOKEN = WORD(PARMS,II)
      IF TOKEN = "" THEN LEAVE
      IF TOKEN = "EMPTY" THEN OPTION = TOKEN
      ELSE IF TOKEN = "RELEASE" THEN RELOPT = "RELEASE"
      ELSE IF SUBSTR(TOKEN,1,1) = "+" | SUBSTR(TOKEN,1,1) = "-"
         THEN DO
            NUMOPT = "CHG"
            NUMCHG = TOKEN
         END
      ELSE IF DATATYPE(TOKEN,'W')
         THEN DO
            NUMOPT = "NEW"
            NUMCHG = TOKEN
         END
      ELSE IF SUBSTR(TOKEN,1,1) = "=",
            | SUBSTR(TOKEN,LENGTH(TOKEN),1) = "="
         THEN ZNEWDSN = TOKEN
      ELSE IF SUBSTR(TOKEN,1,1) = "Q" & DATATYPE(SUBSTR(TOKEN,2),'W')
         THEN Q = SUBSTR(TOKEN,2)
      ELSE DO
         IF ZNEWDSN = "" THEN ZNEWDSN = TOKEN
                         ELSE ZINPDSN = TOKEN
      END
   END II

   IF SUBSTR(ZNEWDSN,1,1) = "=" THEN DO
      IF Q = 0 THEN ZNEWDSN = SUBSTR(ZINPDSN,1,LENGTH(ZINPDSN)-1),
         || SUBSTR(ZNEWDSN,2) || "'"
      ELSE DO
         NN = LENGTH(ZINPDSN) - 1
         DO PP = 1 TO Q
            DO II = NN TO 1 BY -1 WHILE(SUBSTR(ZINPDSN,II,1) <> ".")
            END II
            NN = II - 1
         END PP
         ZNEWDSN = SUBSTR(ZINPDSN,1,NN) || SUBSTR(ZNEWDSN,2) || "'"
      END
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(ZNEWDSN,LENGTH(ZNEWDSN),1) = "=" THEN DO
      IF Q = 0 THEN ZNEWDSN = "'",
         || SUBSTR(ZNEWDSN,1,LENGTH(ZNEWDSN)-1) || SUBSTR(ZINPDSN,2)
      ELSE DO
         NN = 2
         DO PP = 1 TO Q
            DO II = NN TO LENGTH(ZINPDSN)-1,
                  WHILE(SUBSTR(ZINPDSN,II,1) <> ".")
            END II
            NN = II + 1
         END PP
         ZNEWDSN = "'" || SUBSTR(ZNEWDSN,1,LENGTH(ZNEWDSN)-1),
            || SUBSTR(ZINPDSN,NN,LENGTH(ZINPDSN)-NN+1)
      END
   END

   IF LENGTH(ZNEWDSN) > 46 THEN DO
      SAY "***> NEW DATA SET NAME TOO LONG ("ZNEWDSN")"
      EXIT(1)
   END
   IF SYSDSN(ZNEWDSN) = "OK" THEN ADDRESS TSO DELETE ZNEWDSN

   IF OPTION <> "EMPTY" THEN DO
      ADDRESS TSO
      "FREE  DD(SORTIN SORTOUT SYSPRINT SYSIN SORTLIST)"
      LDSI = LISTDSI(ZINPDSN DIRECTORY)
      "ALLOC DD(SORTIN) DSN("ZINPDSN") SHR"
      "ALLOC DD(SYSPRINT) DUMMY"

      IF SYSDSORG = PO THEN DO
         IF SYSADIRBLK = "NO_LIM" THEN DO
            "ALLOC DSN("ZNEWDSN") NEW LIKE("ZINPDSN")" RELOPT,
               "DSNTYPE(LIBRARY) DD(SORTOUT) UNIT(SYSDA)"
            IF RC <> 0 THEN DO
               SAY "***> ALLOCATION FAILED W/ RC =" RC
               SAY "***> UNABLE TO CREATE" ZNEWDSN
               EXIT(1)
            END
         END
         ELSE DO
            IF NUMOPT = "" THEN DO
               "ALLOC DSN("ZNEWDSN") NEW LIKE("ZINPDSN")" RELOPT,
                  "DIR("SYSADIRBLK") DD(SORTOUT) UNIT(SYSDA)"
               IF RC <> 0 THEN DO
                  SAY "***> ALLOCATION FAILED W/ RC =" RC
                  SAY "***> UNABLE TO CREATE" ZNEWDSN
                  EXIT(1)
               END
            END
            ELSE DO
               IF NUMOPT = "NEW" THEN DIRCNT = NUMCHG
               ELSE DIRCNT = SYSADIRBLK + NUMCHG
               IF DIRCNT < SYSUDIRBLK THEN DO
                  SAY "***> NEW NUMBER OF DIRECTORY BLOCKS ("DIRCNT")",
                     "MAY NOT"
                  SAY "***> BE LESS THEN THE NUMBER CURRENTLY IN USE",
                     "("SYSUDIRBLK")"
                  EXIT(1)
               END
               "ALLOC DSN("ZNEWDSN") NEW LIKE("ZINPDSN")" RELOPT,
                  "DIR("DIRCNT") DD(SORTOUT) UNIT(SYSDA)"
               IF RC <> 0 THEN DO
                  SAY "***> ALLOCATION FAILED W/ RC =" RC
                  SAY "***> UNABLE TO CREATE" ZNEWDSN
                  EXIT(1)
               END
            END
         END
         "ALLOC DD(SYSIN) NEW TRACKS SPACE(1) UNIT(SYSDA)",
              " LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(800) RECFM(F B)"
         QUEUE " COPY INDD=SORTIN,OUTDD=SORTOUT"
         "EXECIO" QUEUED() "DISKW SYSIN (FINIS"
         "CALL *(IEBCOPY)"
      END
      ELSE IF SYSDSORG = "PS" | SYSDSORG = "PS-E" THEN DO
         "ALLOC DD(SORTLIST) DUMMY"
         IF NUMOPT = "" THEN DO
            "ALLOC DSN("ZNEWDSN") NEW LIKE("ZINPDSN") DD(SORTOUT)",
               "UNIT(SYSDA)" RELOPT
            IF RC <> 0 THEN DO
               SAY "***> ALLOCATION FAILED W/ RC =" RC
               SAY "***> UNABLE TO CREATE" ZNEWDSN
               EXIT(1)
            END
            "ALLOC DD(SYSIN) NEW TRACKS SPACE(1) UNIT(SYSDA)",
                 "LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(800) RECFM(F B)"
            QUEUE " SORT FIELDS=COPY"
            "EXECIO" QUEUED() "DISKW SYSIN (FINIS"
            "CALL *(SORT)"
            IF RC <> 0 THEN DO
               SAY "***> COPY OF DATA FAILED W/ RC =" RC
               SAY "***> " ZNEWDSN " BUT EMPTY..."
               EXIT(1)
            END
         END
         ELSE DO
            LDSI = LISTDSI(ZINPDSN)
            IF NUMOPT = "NEW" THEN NEWLRECL = NUMCHG
            ELSE NEWLRECL = SYSLRECL + NUMCHG
            IF SYSRECFM = "VB"
               THEN NEWBLKSIZE = SYSBLKSIZE
               ELSE NEWBLKSIZE = NEWLRECL * (27998%NEWLRECL)
            "ALLOC DSN("ZNEWDSN") NEW LIKE("ZINPDSN") DD(SORTOUT)",
               "UNIT(SYSDA)" RELOPT,
               "LRECL("NEWLRECL") BLKSIZE("NEWBLKSIZE")"
            IF RC <> 0 THEN DO
               SAY "***> ALLOCATION FAILED W/ RC =" RC
               SAY "***> UNABLE TO CREATE" ZNEWDSN
               EXIT(1)
            END
            "ALLOC DD(SYSIN) NEW TRACKS SPACE(1) UNIT(SYSDA)",
                 "LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(800) RECFM(F B)"
            QUEUE " SORT FIELDS=COPY "
            IF NEWLRECL > SYSLRECL & INDEX(SYSRECFM,'F') <> 0 THEN DO
               PAD = NEWLRECL - SYSLRECL
               OUTREC_STR = " OUTREC FIELDS=(1," || SYSLRECL,
                  || "," || PAD || "X)"
               QUEUE OUTREC_STR
            END
            "EXECIO" QUEUED() "DISKW SYSIN (FINIS"
            "CALL *(SORT)"
            IF RC <> 0 THEN DO
               SAY "***> COPY OF DATA FAILED W/ RC =" RC
               SAY "***> " ZNEWDSN " BUT EMPTY..."
               EXIT(1)
            END
         END
      END
      "FREE  DD(SORTIN SORTOUT SYSPRINT SYSIN SORTLIST)"
      "ALLOC DD(SYSPRINT) DSN(*)"
      "ALLOC DD(SYSIN) DSN(*)"
   END
   ELSE DO
      ADDRESS TSO
      LDSI = LISTDSI(ZINPDSN DIRECTORY)
      IF SYSDSORG = PO THEN DO
         IF SYSADIRBLK = "NO_LIM" THEN DO
            "ALLOC DSN("ZNEWDSN") NEW LIKE("ZINPDSN")" RELOPT,
               "DSNTYPE(LIBRARY) DD(SORTOUT) UNIT(SYSDA)"
            IF RC <> 0 THEN DO
               SAY "***> ALLOCATION FAILED W/ RC =" RC
               SAY "***> UNABLE TO CREATE" ZNEWDSN
               EXIT(1)
            END
         END
         ELSE DO
            IF NUMOPT = "" THEN DO
               "ALLOC DSN("ZNEWDSN") NEW LIKE("ZINPDSN")" RELOPT,
                  "DIR("SYSADIRBLK") UNIT(SYSDA)"
               IF RC <> 0 THEN DO
                  SAY "***> ALLOCATION FAILED W/ RC =" RC
                  SAY "***> UNABLE TO CREATE" ZNEWDSN
                  EXIT(1)
               END
            END
            ELSE DO
               IF NUMOPT = "NEW" THEN DIRCNT = NUMCHG
               ELSE DIRCNT = SYSADIRBLK + NUMCHG
               "ALLOC DSN("ZNEWDSN") NEW LIKE("ZINPDSN")" RELOPT,
                  "DIR("DIRCNT") DD(SORTOUT) UNIT(SYSDA)"
               IF RC <> 0 THEN DO
                  SAY "***> ALLOCATION FAILED W/ RC =" RC
                  SAY "***> UNABLE TO CREATE" ZNEWDSN
                  EXIT(1)
               END
            END
         END
      END
      ELSE IF SYSDSORG = "PS" | SYSDSORG = "PS-E" THEN DO
         "ALLOC DSN("ZNEWDSN") NEW LIKE("ZINPDSN") UNIT(SYSDA)"
         IF RC <> 0 THEN DO
            SAY "***> ALLOCATION FAILED W/ RC =" RC
            SAY "***> UNABLE TO CREATE" ZNEWDSN
            EXIT(1)
         END
      END
   "FREE  DSN("ZNEWDSN")"
   END

   IF OPTION = "EMPTY"
      THEN SAY ZINPDSN "CLONED TO" ZNEWDSN "WITHOUT COPYING DATA"
      ELSE SAY ZINPDSN "COPIED TO" ZNEWDSN
   EXIT(0)

DISPDOC:
   ADDRESS TSO "CLEAR"
   SAY "                                                             "
   SAY "  CLONER        MAKES A COPY OF A DATA SET UNDER ISPF 3.4    "
   SAY "                SIMILAR TO THE ONE POINTED TO EITHER         "
   SAY "                COPYING THE DATA OR NOT. SIMPLY TYPE 'CLONE' "
   SAY "                FOLLOWED BY THE NEW NAME AND, OPTIONALLY,    "
   SAY "                THE KEYWORD 'EMPTY' AND/OR DIRECTORY COUNT   "
   SAY "                AND/OR THE 'RELEASE' KEYWORD. DELETES ANY    "
   SAY "                EXISTING DATA SET IF IT EXISTS.              "
   SAY "                                                             "
   SAY "  SYNTAX:  CLONER NEW-DATASET-NAME                           "
   SAY "                      <EMPTY>  <#>  <RELEASE>  <Q#>          "
   SAY
   SAY "             NEW-DATASET-NAME   IS THE NAME OF THE DATA SET  "
   SAY "                TO BE CREATED. IT MAY BE QUALIFIED (WITH     "
   SAY "                QUOTES) OR UNQUALIFIED (ASSUMES YOUR USER-   "
   SAY "                ID AT THE FRONT). IT MAY ALSO BE OF THE FORM "
   SAY "                =XXX WHERE XXX IS SUFFIXED TO THE ORIGINAL   "
   SAY "                NAME OR OF THE FORM XXX= WHERE XXX IS        "
   SAY "                PREFIXED TO THE ORIGINAL NAME. THE Q# OPTION "
   SAY "                MAY BE USED TO REMOVE # LEVELS OF QUALIFIERS "
   SAY "                AT THE BACK OR FRONT OF THE ORIGINAL NAME.   "
   SAY
   SAY "            <EMPTY>  IS AN OPTIONAL PARAMETER TO INDICATE    "
   SAY "                NO DATA IS TO BE COPIED FROM THE ORIGINAL    "
   SAY "                FILE.                                        "
   SAY
   SAY "            <#> IS AN OPTIONAL CHANGE TO THE NUMBER OF       "
   SAY "                DIRECTORY BLOCKS IF THE DATA SET IS A PDS.   "
   SAY "                A WHOLE NUMBER IS USED AS IS; PREFIXED BY A +"
   SAY "                IS ADDED; BY A - IS SUBTRACTED. NEVER ALLOWS "
   SAY "                BELOW USED BLOCKS. IF THE DATA SET IS        "
   SAY "                SEQUENTIAL, THE NUMBER BECOMES THE LRECL; A +"
   SAY "                PREFIX ADDS BYTES; A - PREFIX SUBTRACTS.     "
   SAY
   SAY "            <RELEASE> IS AN OPTION THAT WILL RELEASE ANY     "
   SAY "                UNUSED SPACE IN THE RESULTANT FILE           "
   SAY
   SAY "            <Q#> IS AN OPTION TO REMOVE THAT MANY (#) LEVEL  "
   SAY "                QUALIFIERS OF THE ORIGINAL DATA SET EITHER   "
   SAY "                PREFIXING IT WITH THE XXX FROM THE XXX= INPUT"
   SAY "                OR SUFFIXING IT WITH THE XXX FROM THE =XXX.  "
   SAY
   EXIT(1)

./       ADD   NAME=COB2JOB
//GILBERTJ JOB (ACCT#),COB2JOB,                                         00010000
// NOTIFY=&SYSUID,                                                      00020000
// CLASS=A,MSGCLASS=X,COND=(0,NE)                                       00030000
//*                                                                     00040000
//COB2 EXEC PGM=IGYCRCTL                                                00050000
 CBL NOLIB,APOST,NODECK,OBJECT,NOSEQ,BUF(10000),NONAME                  00070000
 CBL NOMAP,NOLIST,NOOFFSET,NOXREF                                       00080000
       Identification Division.                                         00090000
         Program-ID. Cob2Job.                                           00100000
         Author. Gilbert Saint-flour <gsf@pobox.com>.                   00110000
      *----------------------------------------------------------------*00120000
      *                                                                *00130000
      *    This program retrieves specific job-related data from MVS   *00140000
      *    control blocks and moves it to Working-storage.             *00150000
      *                                                                *00160000
      *    The name of the control-block is indicated in pos 1-6 of    *00170000
      *    the Procedure Division lines.                               *00180000
      *    The layout of the MVS control blocks is described in the    *00190000
      *    MVS Data Areas manuals, which can be found on any MVS or    *00200000
      *    OS/390 CD collection or viewed on-line by going to:         *00210000
      *        http://www.s390.ibm.com/bookmgr-cgi/bookmgr.cmd/library *00220000
      *    and searching for:                                          *00230000
      *        MVS DATA AREAS                                          *00240000
      *----------------------------------------------------------------*00250000
       Data Division.                                                   00260000
        Working-Storage Section.                                        00270000
         01 Results.                                                    00280000
           05 job-name Pic x(8).                                        00290000
           05 proc-step Pic x(8).                                       00300000
           05 step-name Pic x(8).                                       00310000
           05 program-name Pic x(8).                                    00320000
           05 program-name2 Pic x(8).                                   00330000
           05 job-number Pic x(8).                                      00340000
           05 job-class Pic x.                                          00350000
           05 msg-class Pic x.                                          00360000
           05 programmer-name Pic x(20).                                00370000
           05 acct1 Pic x(32).                                          00380001
           05 user-id Pic x(8).                                         00390000
           05 group-name Pic x(8).                                      00400000
           05 user-name Pic x(20).                                      00410000
           05 batch-or-cics Pic x(5).                                   00420000
              88 Batch Value 'BATCH'.                                   00430000
              88 CICS  Value 'CICS '.                                   00440000
           05 micro-seconds Pic S9(15) COMP-3.                          00450000
         01 four-bytes.                                                 00460000
           05 full-word Pic s9(8) Comp.                                 00470000
           05 ptr4      Redefines full-word Pointer.                    00480000
        Linkage Section.                                                00490000
         01 cb1.  05 ptr1 Pointer Occurs 256.                           00500000
         01 cb2.  05 ptr2 Pointer Occurs 256.                           00510000
       Procedure Division.                                              00520000
 PSA       SET Address of cb1 to NULL                                   00530000
 TCB       SET Address of cb1 to ptr1(136)                              00540000
           SET ptr4 to ptr1(83)                                         00550000
           COMPUTE micro-seconds = full-word * 1048576                  00560000
           SET ptr4 to ptr1(84)                                         00570000
           COMPUTE micro-seconds = micro-seconds + (full-word / 1024)   00580000
 TIOT      SET Address of cb2 to ptr1(4)                                00590000
           MOVE cb2(1:8) to job-name                                    00600000
           MOVE cb2(9:8) to proc-step                                   00610000
           MOVE cb2(17:8) to step-name                                  00620000
 JSCB      SET Address of cb2 to ptr1(46)                               00630000
           MOVE cb2(361:8) to program-name                              00640000
 SSIB      SET Address of cb2 to ptr2(80)                               00650000
           MOVE cb2(13:8) to job-number                                 00660000
 PRB       SET Address of cb2 to ptr1(1)                                00670000
           MOVE cb2(97:8) to program-name2                              00680000
 JSCB      SET Address of cb2 to ptr1(46)                               00690000
 JCT       SET Address of cb2 to ptr2(66)                               00700000
           MOVE cb2(48:1) to job-class                                  00710000
           MOVE cb2(23:1) to msg-class                                  00720000
 ACT       MOVE zero to full-word                                       00730000
           MOVE cb2(57:3) to four-bytes(2:3)                            00740000
           SET Address of cb2 to ptr4                                   00750000
           MOVE cb2(25:20) to programmer-name                           00760000
           MOVE zero to full-word                                       00770001
           MOVE cb2(49:1) to four-bytes(4:1)                            00780001
           MOVE cb2(50:full-word) to acct1                              00790001
 EXT2      SET Address of cb2 to ptr1(53)                               00800000
 CAUF      IF cb2(21:4) = low-values THEN                               00810000
             SET Batch to TRUE                                          00820000
           ELSE                                                         00830000
             SET CICS to TRUE                                           00840000
           END-IF                                                       00850000
 PSA       SET Address of cb1 to NULL                                   00860000
 ASCB      SET Address of cb1 to ptr1(138)                              00870000
 ASXB      SET Address of cb2 to ptr1(28)                               00880000
           MOVE cb2(193:8) to user-id                                   00890000
 ACEE      SET Address of cb2 to ptr2(51)                               00900000
           MOVE cb2(31:8) to group-name                                 00910000
 UNAM      SET Address of cb1 to ptr2(26)                               00920000
           MOVE zero to full-word                                       00930000
           MOVE cb1(1:1) to four-bytes(4:1)                             00940000
           MOVE cb1(2:full-word) to user-name                           00950000
           DISPLAY job-name ' '                                         00960000
                   proc-step ' '                                        00970000
                   step-name ' '                                        00980000
                   program-name ' '                                     00990000
                   program-name2 ' '                                    01000000
                   job-number ' '                                       01010000
                   job-class ' '                                        01020000
                   msg-class ' '                                        01030000
                   micro-seconds ' '                                    01040000
           DISPLAY quote programmer-name quote ' '                      01050001
                   quote acct1 quote ' '                                01060001
                   batch-or-cics ' '                                    01070000
                   user-id ' '                                          01080000
                   group-name ' '                                       01090001
                   quote user-name quote ' '                            01100001
           GOBACK.                                                      01110000
/*                                                                      01120000
//SYSPRINT DD SYSOUT=*                                                  01130000
//SYSUT1 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      01140000
//SYSUT2 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      01150000
//SYSUT3 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      01160000
//SYSUT4 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      01170000
//SYSUT5 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      01180000
//SYSUT6 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      01190000
//SYSUT7 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      01200000
//SYSLIN DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1),DISP=(,PASS),BLKSIZE=3200            01210000
//*                                                                     01220000
//GOPROC PROC                                                           01230000
//GO    EXEC PGM=LOADER,PARM=PRINT                                      01240000
//SYSLIN DD DSN=*.COB2.SYSLIN,DISP=(OLD,PASS)                           01260000
//SYSLIB DD DSN=CEE.SCEELKED,DISP=SHR                                   01290000
//SYSLOUT DD SYSOUT=*                                                   01300000
//SYSOUT DD SYSOUT=*                                                    01310000
//GOPROC PEND                                                           01320000
//*                                                                     01330000
//GOPROC EXEC GOPROC                                                    01340000
./       ADD   NAME=COB2SYS
//GILBERTS JOB (ACCT#),COB2SYS,                                         00010000
// NOTIFY=&SYSUID,                                                      00020000
// CLASS=A,MSGCLASS=X,COND=(0,NE)                                       00030000
//*                                                                     00040000
//COB2 EXEC PGM=IGYCRCTL                                                00050000
 CBL NOLIB,APOST,NODECK,OBJECT,NOSEQ,BUF(10000),NONAME                  00060000
 CBL NOMAP,NOLIST,NOOFFSET,NOXREF                                       00070000
       Identification Division.                                         00080000
         Program-ID. Cob2Sys.                                           00090000
         Author. Gilbert Saint-flour <gsf@pobox.com>.                   00100000
      *----------------------------------------------------------------*00110000
      *                                                                *00120000
      *    This program retrieves specific system-related data from    *00130000
      *    MVS control blocks and moves it to Working-storage.         *00140000
      *                                                                *00150000
      *    The name of the control-block is indicated in pos 1-6 of    *00160000
      *    the Procedure Division lines.                               *00170000
      *    The layout of the MVS control blocks is described in the    *00180000
      *    MVS Data Areas manuals, which can be found on any MVS or    *00190000
      *    OS/390 CD collection or viewed on-line by going to:         *00200000
      *        http://www.s390.ibm.com/bookmgr-cgi/bookmgr.cmd/library *00210000
      *    and searching for:                                          *00220000
      *        MVS DATA AREAS                                          *00230000
      *                                                                *00240000
      *----------------------------------------------------------------*00250000
       Data Division.                                                   00260000
        Working-Storage Section.                                        00270000
         01 Results.                                                    00280000
           05 sys-name Pic x(8).                                        00290000
           05 real-storage-m Pic s9(6) comp.                            00300000
           05 prodi Pic x(8).                                           00310000
           05 prodn Pic x(8).                                           00320000
           05 mdl Pic 9999.                                             00330000
           05 smf-name Pic x(4).                                        00340000
           05 ipl-jdate Pic 9(7) comp-3.                                00350000
           05 SU-sec Pic s9(6) comp.                                    00360000
           05 cpu-type Pic x(6).                                        00370000
           05 cpu-model Pic x(3).                                       00380000
           05 sysplex-name  Pic x(8).                                   00390000
           05 OS-name    Pic X(16).                                     00400001
           05 OS-release Pic X(6).                                      00410001
           05 hardware-name Pic x(8).                                   00420000
           05 lpar-name Pic x(8).                                       00430000
           05 VM-userid Pic x(8).                                       00440000
         01 four-bytes.                                                 00450000
           05 full-word Pic s9(8) Comp.                                 00460000
           05 ptr4      Redefines full-word Pointer.                    00470000
           05 pl4       Redefines full-word Pic 9(7) comp-3.            00480000
        Linkage Section.                                                00490000
         01 cb1.  05 ptr1 Pointer Occurs 512.                           00500000
         01 cvt.  05 cvt1 Pointer Occurs 512.                           00510000
       Procedure Division.                                              00520000
 PSA       SET ADDRESS OF cb1 TO NULL                                   00530000
 CVT       SET ADDRESS OF cvt TO ptr1(5)                                00540000
           MOVE cvt(341:8) TO sys-name                                  00550000
           MOVE cvt(857:4) TO four-bytes                                00560000
           COMPUTE real-storage-m = (full-word + 1023) / 1024           00570000
           DISPLAY ' SYSNAME='  sys-name                                00580000
           DISPLAY ' STOR='     real-storage-m 'M'                      00590000
CVTFIX     SET ptr4 to ADDRESS OF cvt                                   00600000
           SUBTRACT 256 FROM full-word                                  00610000
           SET ADDRESS OF cb1 TO ptr4                                   00620000
           MOVE cb1(217:8) TO prodi                                     00630000
           MOVE cb1(225:8) TO prodn                                     00640000
           MOVE ZERO to pl4                                             00650000
           MOVE cb1(251:2) TO four-bytes(1:2)                           00660000
           COMPUTE mdl = pl4 / 1000                                     00670000
           DISPLAY ' PRODI=' prodi                                      00680000
           DISPLAY ' PRODN=' prodn                                      00690000
           DISPLAY ' MODEL=' mdl                                        00700000
 SMCA      SET ADDRESS OF cb1 TO cvt1(50)                               00710000
           MOVE cb1(17:4) TO smf-name                                   00720000
           MOVE cb1(341:4) TO four-bytes                                00730000
           COMPUTE ipl-jdate = pl4 + 1900000                            00740000
           DISPLAY ' SMFSID='   smf-name                                00750000
           DISPLAY ' IPL='      ipl-jdate                               00760000
 RMCT      SET ADDRESS OF cb1 TO cvt1(152)                              00770000
           MOVE cb1(65:4) TO four-bytes                                 00780000
           COMPUTE SU-sec = 16000000 / full-word                        00790000
           DISPLAY ' Speed='   SU-sec ' SU/s'                           00800000
 HID       SET ADDRESS OF cb1 TO cvt1(268)                              00810000
           MOVE cb1(27:6) TO cpu-type                                   00820000
           MOVE cb1(33:3) TO cpu-model                                  00830000
           DISPLAY ' CPU='     cpu-type '-' cpu-model                   00840000
 ECVT      SET ADDRESS OF cb1 TO cvt1(36)                               00850000
           MOVE cb1(9:8) TO sysplex-name                                00860000
           MOVE cb1(337:8) TO hardware-name                             00870000
           MOVE cb1(345:8) TO lpar-name                                 00880000
           MOVE cb1(353:8) TO VM-userid                                 00890000
           MOVE cb1(497:16) TO OS-name                                  00900001
           MOVE cb1(513:6) TO OS-release                                00910001
           DISPLAY ' SYSPLEX=' sysplex-name                             00920000
           DISPLAY ' HWNAME='  hardware-name                            00930000
           DISPLAY ' LPAR='    lpar-name                                00940000
           DISPLAY ' VM='      VM-userid                                00950000
           DISPLAY ' OS_Name=' OS-name                                  00960001
           DISPLAY ' Release=' OS-release                               00970001
           GOBACK.                                                      00980000
/*                                                                      00990000
//SYSUT1 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      01000000
//SYSUT2 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      01010000
//SYSUT3 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      01020000
//SYSUT4 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      01030000
//SYSUT5 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      01040000
//SYSUT6 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      01050000
//SYSUT7 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      01060000
//SYSLIN DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1),DISP=(,PASS),BLKSIZE=3200            01070000
//SYSPRINT DD SYSOUT=*                                                  01080000
//*                                                                     01090000
//GO    EXEC PGM=LOADER,PARM=PRINT                                      01100000
//SYSLIN DD DSN=*.COB2.SYSLIN,DISP=(OLD,PASS)                           01110000
//SYSLIB DD DSN=CEE.SCEELKED,DISP=SHR                                   01120000
//SYSLOUT DD SYSOUT=*                                                   01130000
//SYSOUT DD SYSOUT=*                                                    01140000
./       ADD   NAME=COB2TSO
//GILBERTJ JOB (ACCT#),COB2TSO,                                         00010000
// NOTIFY=&SYSUID,                                                      00020000
// CLASS=A,MSGCLASS=X,COND=(0,NE)                                       00030000
//COB2 EXEC PGM=IGYCRCTL                                                00040000
 CBL NOLIB,APOST,NODECK,OBJECT,NOSEQ,BUF(10000),DYNAM                   00050000
 CBL NOMAP,NOLIST,NOOFFSET,NOXREF                                       00060000
      ******************************************************************00070000
      *                                                                *00080000
      *   MODULE NAME = COB2TSO                                        *00090000
      *                                                                *00100000
      *   DESCRIPTIVE NAME = Issue TSO commands from a COBOL program.  *00110000
      *                                                                *00120000
      *   FUNCTION = This sample program demonstrates how to invoke    *00130000
      *              TSO commands from a COBOL program using           *00140000
      *              standard TSO services as documented in the        *00150000
      *              TSO/E Programming Services manual.                *00160000
      *                                                                *00170000
      *              Most TSO commands, including CLISTs and REXX      *00180000
      *              execs can be executed using this technique.       *00190000
      *              TSO commands which require authorization          *00200000
      *              (such as OUTPUT, SEND, TRANSMIT and RECEIVE)      *00210000
      *              will not work.                                    *00220000
      *                                                                *00230000
      *   AUTHOR   =  Gilbert Saint-flour <gsf@pobox.com>              *00240000
      *                                                                *00250000
      ******************************************************************00260000
       Identification Division.                                         00270000
         Program-ID. CB2TSOEV.                                          00280000
                                                                        00290000
       Data Division.                                                   00300000
        Working-Storage Section.                                        00310000
         01 Filler.                                                     00320000
           05 ws-dummy        Pic s9(8) Comp.                           00330000
           05 ws-return-code  Pic s9(8) Comp.                           00340000
           05 ws-reason-code  Pic s9(8) Comp.                           00350000
           05 ws-info-code    Pic s9(8) Comp.                           00360000
           05 ws-cppl-address Pic s9(8) Comp.                           00370000
           05 ws-flags        Pic X(4) Value X'00010001'.               00380000
           05 ws-buffer       Pic X(256).                               00390000
           05 ws-length       Pic s9(8) Comp Value 256.                 00400000
                                                                        00410000
       Procedure Division.                                              00420000
      *----------------------------------------------------------------*00430000
      *          Call IKJTSOEV to create the TSO/E environment         *00440000
      *----------------------------------------------------------------*00450000
           CALL 'IKJTSOEV' Using ws-dummy                               00460000
                                 ws-return-code                         00470000
                                 ws-reason-code                         00480000
                                 ws-info-code                           00490000
                                 ws-cppl-address.                       00500000
           IF ws-return-code > zero                                     00510000
             DISPLAY 'IKJTSOEV Failed, Return-code=' ws-return-code     00520000
                                     ' Reason-code=' ws-reason-code     00530000
                                     'Info-code='    ws-info-code       00540000
             MOVE ws-return-code to Return-code                         00550000
             STOP RUN.                                                  00560000
      *----------------------------------------------------------------*00570000
      *          Build the TSO/E command in ws-buffer                  *00580000
      *----------------------------------------------------------------*00590000
                                                                        00600000
           MOVE 'ALLOCATE DD(SYSPUNCH) SYSOUT HOLD' to ws-buffer.       00610000
                                                                        00620000
      *----------------------------------------------------------------*00630000
      *   Call the TSO/E Service Routine to execute the TSO/E command  *00640000
      *----------------------------------------------------------------*00650000
           CALL 'IKJEFTSR' Using ws-flags                               00660000
                                 ws-buffer                              00670000
                                 ws-length                              00680000
                                 ws-return-code                         00690000
                                 ws-reason-code                         00700000
                                 ws-dummy.                              00710000
           IF ws-return-code > zero                                     00720000
             DISPLAY 'IKJEFTSR Failed, Return-code=' ws-return-code     00730000
                                     ' Reason-code=' ws-reason-code     00740000
             MOVE ws-return-code to Return-code                         00750000
             STOP RUN.                                                  00760000
                                                                        00770000
      *----------------------------------------------------------------*00780000
      *          Check that the ALLOCATE command worked                *00790000
      *----------------------------------------------------------------*00800000
           DISPLAY 'ALLOCATE Worked ! ' Upon Syspunch.                  00810000
                                                                        00820000
           STOP RUN.                                                    00830000
/*                                                                      00840000
//SYSPRINT DD SYSOUT=*                                                  00850000
//SYSUT1 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      00860000
//SYSUT2 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      00870000
//SYSUT3 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      00880000
//SYSUT4 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      00890000
//SYSUT5 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      00900000
//SYSUT6 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      00910000
//SYSUT7 DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1)                                      00920000
//SYSLIN DD UNIT=VIO,SPACE=(TRK,1),DISP=(,PASS),BLKSIZE=3200            00930000
//*                                                                     00940000
//GO    EXEC PGM=LOADER,PARM=NOPRINT                                    00950000
//SYSLIN DD DSN=*.COB2.SYSLIN,DISP=(OLD,PASS)                           00960000
//SYSLIB DD DSN=CEE.SCEELKED,DISP=SHR                                   00970000
//SYSOUT DD SYSOUT=*                                                    00980000
//SYSTSPRT DD SYSOUT=*                                                  00990000
./       ADD   NAME=COMPRS
/**  REXX -- COMPRESS THE PDS EDITED OR ONE SPECIFIED  **/

   ADDRESS 'ISPEXEC'
   "ISREDIT MACRO (DSN)"
   IF RC > 0 THEN EXIT(RC)
   "ISREDIT ("SAVLINE","SAVCOL") = CURSOR "
   SAVEMSG = MSG("OFF")

   UPPER DSN
   IF DSN = '?' THEN SIGNAL DISPDOC
   IF DSN = '' THEN DO
      "ISREDIT (DSN) = DATASET"
      DSN = "'" || DSN || "'"
   END

   ADDRESS TSO
   "FREE  DD(SYSUT1 SYSPRINT SYSIN)"
   "ALLOC DD(SYSUT1) DSN("DSN") SHR"
   "ALLOC DD(SYSPRINT) DUMMY"
   "ALLOC DD(SYSIN) NEW TRACKS SPACE(1) UNIT(SYSDA)",
        " LRECL(80) BLKSIZE(800) RECFM(F B)"
   QUEUE " COPY INDD=SYSUT1,OUTDD=SYSUT1"
   "EXECIO" QUEUED() "DISKW SYSIN (FINIS"
   "CALL *(IEBCOPY)"
   RETCODE = RC
   "FREE  DD(SYSUT1 SYSPRINT SYSIN)"
   "ALLOC DD(SYSPRINT) DSN(*)"

   STR = 'COMPRESSED RC='RETCODE
   CALL SETMSG '* NO ' STR ' DONE $PDS' DSN 'COMPRESSED...'
   "ISREDIT LOCATE" SAVLINE
   "ISREDIT CURSOR = "SAVLINE SAVCOL
   IF SAVEMSG = 'ON' THEN
      X = MSG("ON")
   RETURN RETCODE

SETMSG:
   PARSE ARG ZERRHM ZERRALRM ZERRSM'$'ZERRLM
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC 'SETMSG MSG(ISRZ002) COND'
   RETURN


DISPDOC:
   ADDRESS TSO "CLEAR"
   SAY "COMPRESS - CURRENT PDS OR SPECIFIED ONE                   "
   SAY
   SAY " FORMAT "
   SAY
   SAY "    COMPRESS  ( PDS-NAME )                                "
   SAY
   SAY "       INVOKE IEBCOPY COMPRESS AGAINST EITHER THE CURRENT "
   SAY "       (DEFAULTED WHEN NO PDS-NAME SPECIFIED) OR THE      "
   SAY "       DATA SET SPECIFIED.                                "
   SAY
   SAY " EXAMPLE "
   SAY
   SAY "    COMPRESS  'USERID.TEST.MACLIB'                        "
   SAY
   SAY "       WILL COMPRESS 'USERID.TEST.MACLIB'                 "
   SAY
   EXIT(1)

./       ADD   NAME=CONCATDD
/**  REXX -- CONCATENATE A DATA SET TO A DDNAME                    **/
/*                                                                  */
/* SYNTAX FOR INVOKING THIS CLIST IS:                               */
/*    CONCATDD DDNAME DATA.SET.NAME   (TO PUT IT AT THE BEGINNING)  */
/*    CONCATDD DDNAME DATA.SET.NAME B (TO PUT IT AT THE END)        */
/*       NOTE NO QUOTES ON THE DATA SET NAME!                       */
/********************************************************************/
   PARSE  UPPER  ARG  DDNAME  DSNAME  B
   X = MSG("OFF")
   IF SUBSTR(DDNAME,1,1) = '?' THEN SIGNAL DISPDOC
   IF SYSDSN("'"DSNAME"'") ¬= 'OK' THEN DO
       SAY  DSNAME 'DOES NOT EXIST OR ISN''T CATALOGED'
       EXIT
    END
   X = OUTTRAP("TRAP.","*")
   "LISTALC STATUS"
   X= OUTTRAP("OFF")

   FOUND = 'NO'
   DO  II  =  1  TO  TRAP.0  WHILE  FOUND <> 'YES'
      DSN = TRAP.II
      IF SUBSTR(DSN,1,10) = '  ' || DDNAME THEN DO
         FOUND   = 'YES'
         JJ  = II - 1
         DSN = TRAP.JJ
         IF DSN <> DSNAME THEN CONCAT = "'" || DSN || "'"
      END
   END

   IF  FOUND = 'YES' THEN DO
      DO JJ = (II+1) TO (TRAP.0) BY 2
         DSN = TRAP.JJ
         IF SUBSTR(DSN,3,8) = ' ' THEN DO
            KK = JJ - 1
            DSN = TRAP.KK
            IF DSN <> DSNAME THEN CONCAT = CONCAT || " '" || DSN || "'"
         END
         ELSE JJ = TRAP.0 +100
      END
   END
   ELSE DO
      SAY 'DDNAME' DDNAME 'NOT CURRENTLY ALLOCATED'
      EXIT
   END

   DSNBOT = ''
   DSNTOP = ''
   IF B = 'B' THEN DSNBOT = "'" || DSNAME || "'"
              ELSE DSNTOP = "'" || DSNAME || "'"
   "ALLOC DD("DDNAME") DSN("DSNTOP CONCAT DSNBOT") SHR REU"
   EXIT(0)

DISPDOC:
   ADDRESS TSO "CLEAR"
   SAY "CONCATDD - CONCATENATE A DATA SET TO A DD NAME            "
   SAY
   SAY " FORMAT "
   SAY
   SAY "    CONCATDD  DDNAME  DSNAME  ( B | T )                   "
   SAY
   SAY "       WILL ADD THE DATA SET TO THE TOP OR BOTTOM OF THE  "
   SAY "       DD NAME'S CONCATENATION. THE DATA SET NAME MUST BE "
   SAY "       IN SINGLES QUOTES. 'T' FOR TOP IS THE DEFAULT      "
   SAY
   SAY "       WILL CHECK IF THE DATA SET EXISTS AND WHETHER THE  "
   SAY "       DD NAME IS ALLOCATED. WILL MOVE THE DATA SET TO    "
   SAY "       THE TOP OR BOTTOM, AS SPECIFIED, IF ALREADY IN THE "
   SAY "       CONCATENATION.                                     "
   SAY
   EXIT(1)

./       ADD   NAME=CU
/**  REXX -- CREATE CLEAN UP JCL AFTER CURSOR POSITION  **/
   SUBCOM ISPEXEC
   IF RC <> 0 THEN DO
      SAY 'CU EDIT MACRO CAN ONLY BE RUN UNDER ISPF EDIT!'
      EXIT(12)
   END
   SUBCOM ISREDIT
   IF RC = 0 THEN DO
      ADDRESS ISREDIT "ISREDIT MACRO (PARMS) NOPROCESS"
      PARMS = TRANSLATE(PARMS)
      IF PARMS = "?" THEN SIGNAL DISPDOC
   END
   ELSE DO
      SAY 'CU EDIT MACRO CAN ONLY BE RUN UNDER ISPF EDIT!'
      EXIT(12)
   END
   IF DATATYPE(PARMS,'W') THEN NUMDELS = PARMS
                          ELSE NUMDELS = 1

   ADDRESS ISREDIT
   "(LINE,COL) = CURSOR"
   IF LINE = 1  THEN DO
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "VGET (ZSCREENC,ZSCREENI) SHARED"
       II = INDEX(ZSCREENI,'* Top of Data *')
       IF ( ZSCREENC % 80 )  <=  ( II % 80 )  THEN LINE = 0
       ELSE LINE = 1
   END
   DDNUM = NUMDELS
   CARD1 = "//***"
   "LINE_AFTER (LINE) = (CARD1)"
   CARD2 = "//             DISP=(MOD,DELETE,DELETE),",
      || "UNIT=SYSDA,SPACE=(TRK,0)"
   CARD1 = "//DEL001       DD       DSN=...,"
   DO II = 1 TO NUMDELS
      "LINE_AFTER (LINE) = (CARD2)"
      PATCH = RIGHT(DDNUM,3,'0')
      DDNUM = DDNUM - 1
      CARD1 = OVERLAY(PATCH,CARD1,6,3)
      "LINE_AFTER (LINE) = (CARD1)"
   END II
   CARD1 = "//CLEANUP    EXEC     PGM=IEFBR14"
   "LINE_AFTER (LINE) = (CARD1)"
   CARD1 = "//***"
   "LINE_AFTER (LINE) = (CARD1)"
   LINE = LINE + 3
   COL  = 29
   "CURSOR = " LINE COL
   EXIT(0)

DISPDOC:
   ADDRESS TSO "CLEAR"
   SAY "CU  -  COPY CLEAN UP JCL AFTER CURSOR POSITION            "
   SAY
   SAY " FORMAT "
   SAY
   SAY "    CU  ( ### ) ( ? )                                     "
   SAY
   SAY "       CREATE AN IEFBR14 WITH ### MOD/DELETE CARDS AFTER  "
   SAY "       THE CURSOR POSITION. ### DEFAULTS TO 1.            "
   SAY
   SAY "       A QUESTION MARK ALONE CAUSES THIS HELP TO DISPLAY. "
   SAY
   EXIT(1)

./       ADD   NAME=CUD
/** REXX -- DYNAMICALLY CREATE CLEAN UP JCL AFTER CURSOR POSITION **/
   SUBCOM ISPEXEC
   IF RC <> 0 THEN DO
      SAY 'CUD EDIT MACRO CAN ONLY BE RUN UNDER ISPF EDIT!'
      EXIT(12)
   END
   SUBCOM ISREDIT
   IF RC = 0 THEN DO
      ADDRESS ISREDIT "ISREDIT MACRO (PARMS) NOPROCESS"
      PARMS = TRANSLATE(PARMS)
      IF PARMS = "?" THEN SIGNAL DISPDOC
   END
   ELSE DO
      SAY 'CUD EDIT MACRO CAN ONLY BE RUN UNDER ISPF EDIT!'
      EXIT(12)
   END

   ADDRESS ISREDIT
   "(LINE,COL) = CURSOR"
   IF LINE = 1  THEN DO
       ADDRESS ISPEXEC "VGET (ZSCREENC,ZSCREENI) SHARED"
       II = INDEX(ZSCREENI,'* Top of Data *')
       IF ( ZSCREENC % 80 )  <=  ( II % 80 )  THEN LINE = 0
       ELSE LINE = 1
   END
   "PROCESS RANGE C"
   IF RC > 0 THEN DO
      "(TOP) = LINENUM .ZFIRST"
      "(BOT) = LINENUM .ZLAST"
   END
   ELSE DO
      "(TOP) = LINENUM .ZFRANGE"
      "(BOT) = LINENUM .ZLRANGE"
   END

   CARD4 = "//           DISP=(MOD,DELETE,DELETE),",
      || "UNIT=TEST,SPACE=(TRK,0)"
   CARD3 = "//DEL...     DD    DSN="
   CARD2 = "//CLEANUP  EXEC  PGM=IEFBR14"
   CARD1 = "//***"

   ARRAY.0 = 0
   DO II = TOP TO BOT
      "ISREDIT (REC) = LINE &II"
      IF (POS('DISP=(,CAT',REC) <> 0 | POS('DISP=(NEW,CAT',REC) <> 0),
            & SUBSTR(REC,1,3) <> '//*' THEN DO
         JJ = POS('DSN=',REC)
         IF JJ = 0 THEN DO
            JJ = POS('DSNAME=',REC)
            IF JJ <> 0 THEN JJ = JJ + 3
         END
         IF JJ = 0 THEN DO
            XX = II - 1
            "ISREDIT (REC) = LINE &XX"
            DO WHILE(SUBSTR(REC,1,3) = '//*' | SUBSTR(REC,1,2) = '/*')
               XX = XX - 1
               "ISREDIT (REC) = LINE &XX"
            END
            DO KK = 71 TO 1 BY -1 WHILE(SUBSTR(REC,KK,1) = ' ')
            END KK
            DO WHILE(SUBSTR(REC,KK,1) = ',')
               JJ = POS('DSN=',REC)
               IF JJ = 0 THEN DO
                  JJ = POS('DSNAME=',REC)
                  IF JJ <> 0 THEN JJ = JJ + 3
               END
               IF JJ <> 0 THEN LEAVE
               XX = XX - 1
               "ISREDIT (REC) = LINE &XX"
               DO WHILE(SUBSTR(REC,1,3) = '//*')
                  XX = XX - 1
                  "ISREDIT (REC) = LINE &XX"
               END
               DO KK = 71 TO 1 BY -1 WHILE(SUBSTR(REC,KK,1) = ' ')
               END KK
            END
            IF JJ = 0 THEN DO
               XX = II
               "ISREDIT (REC) = LINE &XX"
               DO KK = 71 TO 1 BY -1 WHILE(SUBSTR(REC,KK,1) = ' ')
               END KK
               DO WHILE(SUBSTR(REC,KK,1) = ',')
                  XX = XX + 1
                  "ISREDIT (REC) = LINE &XX"
                  DO WHILE(SUBSTR(REC,1,3) = '//*')
                     XX = XX + 1
                     "ISREDIT (REC) = LINE &XX"
                  END
                  JJ = POS('DSN=',REC)
                  IF JJ = 0 THEN DO
                     JJ = POS('DSNAME=',REC)
                     IF JJ <> 0 THEN JJ = JJ + 3
                  END
                  IF JJ <> 0 THEN LEAVE
                  DO KK = 71 TO 1 BY -1 WHILE(SUBSTR(REC,KK,1) = ' ')
                  END KK
               END
            END
         END
         IF JJ <> 0 THEN DO
            JJ = JJ + 4
            DO KK = (JJ+1) TO 71,
               WHILE(SUBSTR(REC,KK,1) <> ' ' & SUBSTR(REC,KK,1) <> ',')
            END KK
            IF SUBSTR(REC,kk-1,1) <> ')' THEN DO
               ARRAY.0 = ARRAY.0 + 1
               NN      = ARRAY.0
               ARRAY.NN = SUBSTR(REC,JJ,KK-JJ)
            END
         END
      END
   END II

   IF ARRAY.0 > 0 THEN "LINE_AFTER (LINE) = (CARD1)"
   DO II = ARRAY.0 TO 1 BY -1
      "LINE_AFTER (LINE) = (CARD4)"
      CARD  = CARD3 || ARRAY.II || ','
      PATCH = RIGHT(II,3,'0')
      CARD  = OVERLAY(PATCH,CARD,6,3)
      "LINE_AFTER (LINE) = (CARD)"
   END II

   IF ARRAY.0 > 0 THEN DO
      "LINE_AFTER (LINE) = (CARD2)"
      "LINE_AFTER (LINE) = (CARD1)"
   END
   ELSE SAY "No 'NEW,CATLG' dispositions found; no JCL generated!"

   IF LINE = 0 AND COL = 0 THEN EXIT(1)
   ELSE DO
      'ISREDIT CURSOR = ' LINE COL
      EXIT(0)
   END

DISPDOC:
   ADDRESS TSO "CLEAR"
   SAY "CUD  -  DYNAMICALLY GENERATE CLEAN UP JCL AFTER CURSOR    "
   SAY
   SAY " FORMAT "
   SAY
   SAY "    CUD  ( ? )                                            "
   SAY
   SAY "       CREATE AN IEFBR14 WITH MOD/DELETE CARDS FOR EVERY  "
   SAY "       NEW CATALOGED DATA SET IN THE FILE AND PLACE THEM  "
   SAY "       IMMEDIATELY AFTER WHERE THE CURSOR IS POSITIONED.  "
   SAY "       C/CC/C# MAY BE USED TO LIMIT THE SEARCH.           "
   SAY
   SAY "       A QUESTION MARK ALONE CAUSES THIS HELP TO DISPLAY. "
   SAY
   EXIT(1)

./       ADD   NAME=DATE11
/**  REXX -- Show Today's Date  **/
   ARG PARMS
   IF SUBSTR(PARMS,1,1) = '?' THEN SIGNAL DISPDOC

   SAY 'DATE(S) IS : ' DATE(S)
   IF PARMS = '' THEN DO
      DD = SUBSTR(DATE(U),4,2)
      IF SUBSTR(DD,2,1) = '1'         THEN XX = 'st'
         ELSE IF SUBSTR(DD,2,1) = '2' THEN XX = 'nd'
         ELSE IF SUBSTR(DD,2,1) = '3' THEN XX = 'rd'
         ELSE XX = 'th'
      IF SUBSTR(DD,1,1) = '0'         THEN DD = SUBSTR(DD,2)
      LILIAN = DATE('B') - 577734
      $LILIAN = ""
      DO JJ = 3 TO 21 BY 3 WHILE JJ < LENGTH(LILIAN)
         $LILIAN = "," || SUBSTR(LILIAN,LENGTH(LILIAN)-JJ+1,3),
            || $LILIAN
      END
      $LILIAN = SUBSTR(LILIAN,1,LENGTH(LILIAN)+3-JJ) || $LILIAN
      SAY DATE(W) DATE(M) DD||XX',' SUBSTR(DATE(S),1,4),
         '(day' SUBSTR(DATE(J),3,3)') Lillian('$LILIAN')'
      Exit(0)
   END
   IF LENGTH(PARMS) < 7 | LENGTH(PARMS) > 8 THEN SIGNAL DISPDOC
   IF ¬DATATYPE(PARMS,'W') THEN SIGNAL DISPDOC
   IF LENGTH(PARMS) = 7 THEN DO
      SPARMS = DATE(S,SUBSTR(PARMS,3),J)
      IF SUBSTR(SPARMS,8,1) = '1'         THEN XX = 'st'
         ELSE IF SUBSTR(SPARMS,8,1) = '2' THEN XX = 'nd'
         ELSE IF SUBSTR(SPARMS,8,1) = '3' THEN XX = 'rd'
         ELSE XX = 'th'
      IF SUBSTR(SPARMS,7,2) = '11'         THEN XX = 'th'
         ELSE IF SUBSTR(SPARMS,7,2) = '12' THEN XX = 'th'
         ELSE IF SUBSTR(SPARMS,7,2) = '13' THEN XX = 'th'

      DD = SUBSTR(SPARMS,7,2)
      IF SUBSTR(DD,1,1) = '0'             THEN DD = SUBSTR(DD,2)
      LL = DD' 'SUBSTR(DATE(M,SPARMS,S),1,3)' 'SUBSTR(PARMS,1,4)
      LILIAN = DATE('B',LL) - 577734
      $LILIAN = ""
      DO JJ = 3 TO 21 BY 3 WHILE JJ < LENGTH(LILIAN)
         $LILIAN = "," || SUBSTR(LILIAN,LENGTH(LILIAN)-JJ+1,3),
            || $LILIAN
      END
      $LILIAN = SUBSTR(LILIAN,1,LENGTH(LILIAN)+3-JJ) || $LILIAN
      SAY DATE(W,SPARMS,S) DATE(M,SPARMS,S) DD||XX',',
         SUBSTR(PARMS,1,4) '(day' SUBSTR(PARMS,5,3)')',
         ' Lillian('$LILIAN')'
   END
   ELSE DO
      IF SUBSTR(PARMS,8,1) = '1'         THEN XX = 'st'
         ELSE IF SUBSTR(PARMS,8,1) = '2' THEN XX = 'nd'
         ELSE IF SUBSTR(PARMS,8,1) = '3' THEN XX = 'rd'
         ELSE XX = 'th'
      IF SUBSTR(PARMS,7,2) = '11'         THEN XX = 'th'
         ELSE IF SUBSTR(PARMS,7,2) = '12' THEN XX = 'th'
         ELSE IF SUBSTR(PARMS,7,2) = '13' THEN XX = 'th'

      DD = SUBSTR(PARMS,7,2)
      IF SUBSTR(DD,1,1) = '0'            THEN DD = SUBSTR(DD,2)
      LL = DD' 'SUBSTR(DATE(M,PARMS,S),1,3)' 'SUBSTR(PARMS,1,4)
      LILIAN = DATE('B',LL) - 577734
      $LILIAN = ""
      DO JJ = 3 TO 21 BY 3 WHILE JJ < LENGTH(LILIAN)
         $LILIAN = "," || SUBSTR(LILIAN,LENGTH(LILIAN)-JJ+1,3),
            || $LILIAN
      END
      $LILIAN = SUBSTR(LILIAN,1,LENGTH(LILIAN)+3-JJ) || $LILIAN
      SAY DATE(W,PARMS,S) DATE(M,PARMS,S) DD||XX',',
         SUBSTR(PARMS,1,4) '(day' RIGHT(DATE(D,PARMS,S),3,'0')')',
         ' Lillian('$LILIAN')'
   END
   Exit(0)

./       ADD   NAME=DCVHDATE
/* rexx */                                                              00010000
/*    PURPOSE:      To set the control file allocated to DATEDD to     =00020000
=                   the next day                                       =00030000
=                                                                      =00040000
=     AUTHOR:       Rama .J                                            =00050000
=                                                                      =00060000
=     DATE:         November 2007                                      =00070000
=                                                                      =00080000
=     SYNTAX:       LMTHDATE  format-id                                =00090000
=                                                                      =00100000
=     PARAMETERS:   format-id                                          =00110000
=                      - CA     =>   yyyy-mm-dd                        =00120000
=                      - CA8    =>   yy-mm-dd                          =00130000
=                      - UK     =>   dd/mm/yyyy                        =00140000
=                      - UK8    =>   dd/mm/yy                          =00150000
=                      - US     =>   mm/dd/yyyy                        =00160000
=                      - US8    =>   mm/dd/yy                          =00170000
=                      - ORD    =>   yy/mm/dd                          =00180000
=                      - default = US8                                 =00190000
=                                                                      =00200000
=     INPUT:        none                                               =00210000
=                                                                      =00220000
=     OUTPUT:                                                          =00230000
=       file(ddname) = DATEDD                                          =00240000
=                      - a member of a PDS/library or a sequential file=00250000
=                                                                      =00260000
=       Return code                                                    =00270000
=                    0  -  file written OK                             =00280000
=                    4  -  invalid format specified, default used      =00290000
=                    8  -  cannot open file                            =00300000
=                   12  -  I/O error writing file                      =00310000

 k_lastdayl = "31 29 31 30 31 30 31 31 30 31 30 31"                     00400000

 IF  Length(trc) = 1  THEN  TRACE Value trc                             00430000
 dflt.format = "US8"                                                    00440000
 maxrc = 0                                                              00450000

/*  Find the last day of the Month                                    */00581015
                                                                        00581115
 IF leapyear(yyyy)                                                      00581215

     dd1 = word(k_lastdayl,mm)                                          00581415
             END                                                        00581515

     dd1 = word(k_lastday,mm)                                           00581715
             END                                                        00581815

/*====================================================================  00582315
=   If Today is last day of the month , change dd = 01 & mm = mm + 1 =  00582416
=   If Today is last day of the year                                 =  00582516
=   Change mm = 01 yyyy = yyyy + 1 and dd = 01                       =  00582616
=   Otherwise Just Increment the date                                =  00582716
= ====================================================================*/00582816
                                                                        00582915
 IF  dd = dd1                                                           00583015
        THEN DO                                                         00583115
    IF  mm = "12"                                                       00583200
          THEN DO                                                       00584000
            mm = "01"                                                   00585000
            dd = "01"                                                   00585105
            yyyy = yyyy + 1                                             00586000
               END                                                      00587000
          ELSE DO                                                       00588000
            mm = mm + 1                                                 00589000
            mm = RIGHT(mm,2,'0')                                        00590000
            dd = "01"                                                   00600000
               END                                                      00610000
             END                                                        00620000
 ELSE DO                                                                00630000
     dd = dd + 1                                                        00640000
     dd = RIGHT(dd,2,'0')                                               00650000
      END                                                               00660000
 PARSE  VALUE yyyy WITH cc 3 yr                                         00670000

 SELECT                                                                 00690000
   WHEN  format = "ORD"  THEN  res = yr"/"mm"/"dd                       00700000
   WHEN  format = "CA8"  THEN  res = yr"-"mm"-"dd                       00710000
   WHEN  format = "UK8"  THEN  res = dd"/"mm"/"yr                       00720000
   WHEN  format = "US8"  THEN  res = mm"/"dd"/"yr                       00730000

   WHEN  format = "UK"  THEN  res = dd"/"mm"/"yyyy                      00750000
   OTHERWISE /* format = "US" */  res = mm"/"dd"/"yyyy                  00760000
   END                                                                  00770000

 IF maxrc <= 4                                                          00790000
