./       ADD   NAME=RJUST
/**  REXX -- RIGHT JUSTIFIES DATA USING CC/C## RANGE OR DEFAULT TO **/
/*        FILE; WILL ACCEPT BOUNDARIES AS PARMS OR USE ISPF BOUNDS  */

   SAVEMSG = MSG()
   X = MSG("OFF")
   X = ADDRESS()
   SUBCOM ISPEXEC
   IF RC <> 0 THEN DO
      SAY "RJUST MUST BE RUN UNDER ISPF EDIT!"
      SIGNAL QUIT
      END
   SUBCOM ISREDIT
   UMODE = "ISREDIT"
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "CONTROL ERRORS RETURN"
   ADDRESS ISREDIT
   "MACRO (LEFT,RIGHT) NOPROCESS"
   IF LEFT = '?' THEN SIGNAL DISPDOC

   IF LEFT <> "" AND RIGHT = "" THEN DO
      "ISREDIT (L2,RIGHT) = BOUNDS"
      END

   "PROCESS RANGE C"
   IF RC > 0 THEN DO
      "(TOP) = LINENUM .ZFIRST"
      "(BOT) = LINENUM .ZLAST"
   END
   ELSE DO
      "(TOP) = LINENUM .ZFRANGE"
      "(BOT) = LINENUM .ZLRANGE"
   END

   "ISREDIT("LB","RB") = BOUNDS"
   IF LEFT  <> "" THEN LB = LEFT
   IF RIGHT <> "" THEN RB = RIGHT

   DO II = TOP TO BOT BY 1
      "ISREDIT (RECORD) = LINE &II"
      DO JJ = RB TO LB BY -1 WHILE(SUBSTR(RECORD,JJ,1) = ' ')
         END
      IF RB > JJ THEN DO
         RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,LB-1)  || SUBSTR(RECORD,JJ+1,RB-JJ),
            || SUBSTR(RECORD,LB,JJ-LB+1) || SUBSTR(RECORD,RB+1)
         "ISREDIT LINE &II = &STR(RECORD)"
         END
      END

QUIT:
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC
   X = MSG(SAVEMSG)
   ADDRESS ISREDIT "LOCATE" TOP
   EXIT(1)

DISPDOC:
   ADDRESS TSO "CLEAR"
   SAY "RJUST - RIGHT JUSTIFY TEXT W/IN BOUNDS                   "
   SAY
   SAY " FORMAT "
   SAY
   SAY "    RJUST   ( LEFT-COLUMN  RIGHT-COLUMN )                "
   SAY
   SAY "       WILL CAUSE THE MARKED (VIA C/CC/C##) RANGE OF     "
   SAY "       LINES TO BE RIGHT JUSTIFIED WITHIN THE BOUNDS THEN"
   SAY "       IN FORCE.  IF NO RANGE IS SPECIFIED, THE ENTIRE   "
   SAY "       FILE IS PROCESSED.  THE FIRST AND THE LAST        "
   SAY "       NON-BLANK CHARACTERS WITHIN THE BOUNDS DETERMINE  "
   SAY "       THE SIZE OF THE DATA TO BE RIGHT JUSTIFIED.       "
   SAY "       SPECIFYING A LEFT COLUMN AND RIGHT COLUMN WILL    "
   SAY "       CAUSE ONLY THE DATA IN THOSE COLUMNS TO BE        "
   SAY "       JUSTIFIED.                                        "
   SAY
   SAY " EXAMPLE "
   SAY
   SAY "    RJUST  1 50                                          "
   SAY "       WILL CAUSE THE TEST IN COLUMNS 1 THRU 50 TO BE    "
   SAY "       SHIFTED RIGHT SO THAT THE LAST NON BLANK IN THOSE "
   SAY "       COLUMNS WILL BE IN POSITION 50.                   "
   SAY
   EXIT(1)

./       ADD   NAME=SJ
/* Rexx Custom Submit */
"isredit macro"
address ispexec
'isredit (openmbr) = member'
'isredit (opendsn) = dataset'
call outtrap 'out.'
address tso "submit '"opendsn'('openmbr')'"'"
call outtrap 'off'
do i = 1 to out.0
   parse var out.i 'JOB' jobname '(' jobid ')' status
end i
subjobname = strip(jobname,b)
subjobid   = strip(jobid,b)
subjob     = subjobname || "(" || subjobid || ")"
say out.1
"isredit locate .zfirst"
"isredit change p'========'" subjobid "65 72"
"isredit locate 0"
"isredit cursor = " 1 1
exit 1
./       ADD   NAME=SJ1
   /* REXX */
    XDSN = 'JONNALR.TEST.JCL(DELETE)'
    'ISPEXEC VIEW DATASET('XDSN')'
    ADDRESS ISREDIT
    ISREDIT "CHANGE ALL 'EXTRACT' 'EXTRACT1'"
    ISREDIT  "SUB"
    ISREDIT  "CANCEL"
    ISREDIT  "END"
    EXIT
./       ADD   NAME=SKEL1
 /*REXX*/
 arg NEWDS OLDDS
 if (NEWDS = '') then do
    say "Missing New file name - to be created"
    exit
 end
 if (OLDDS = '') then do
    say "Missing Existing file name - to be cloned"
    exit
 end
 /* Look at the current CLIST dataset for skeletons */
 "ispexec libdef ispslib library id(sysproc)"
 /* ISPEXEC LIBDEF ISPPLIB DATASET ID('SYS1.OPC.SEQQPNL0') */
 /* open the skeleton and output to temp dataset */
 "ispexec ftopen temp"
 "ispexec ftincl DSCLONE"  /*DSCLONE is where the skeleton jcl lies*/
 /* close the output */
 "ispexec ftclose"
 "ispexec vget (ztempf) shared"
 /*submits JCL at temp dataset */
 "submit '"ztempf"'"
 exit
./       ADD   NAME=SQUSH
/**  REXX -- LEFT JUSTIFIES DATA AND TURNS MULTIPLE BLANKS INTO ONE **/

   ADDRESS ISREDIT
   "MACRO (LEFT,RIGHT) NOPROCESS"

   IF LEFT = "?" THEN SIGNAL DISPDOC
   IF LEFT <> "" AND RIGHT = "" THEN DO
      "ISREDIT (L2,RIGHT) = BOUNDS"
      END

   "PROCESS RANGE C"
   IF RC = 0 THEN DO
      "(FIRST) = LINENUM .ZFRANGE"
      "(LAST)  = LINENUM .ZLRANGE"
   END
   ELSE DO
      "(FIRST) = LINENUM .ZFIRST"
      "(LAST)  = LINENUM .ZLAST"
   END

   "ISREDIT ("LB","RB") = BOUNDS"
   IF LEFT  <> "" THEN LB = LEFT
   IF RIGHT <> "" THEN RB = RIGHT
   "ISREDIT ("LRECL")   = LRECL"

   DO II = FIRST TO LAST
      "(LINE) = LINE " II
      IF LB = 1 & RB = LRECL THEN DO
         SELECT
            WHEN WORDS(LINE) = 0 THEN NOP
            OTHERWISE LINE = SPACE(LINE)
         END  /*** END OF SELECT ***/
      END
      ELSE DO
         BLOCK = SUBSTR(LINE,LB,RB-LB+1)
         SELECT
            WHEN WORDS(BLOCK) = 0 THEN NOP
            OTHERWISE BLOCK = SPACE(BLOCK)
         END  /*** END OF SELECT ***/
         LINE = SUBSTR(LINE,1,LB-1) || BLOCK,
            || COPIES(' ',RB-LB+1-LENGTH(BLOCK)),
            || SUBSTR(LINE,RB+1)
      END
      "LINE "II"= (LINE)"
   END II

   "LOCATE" FIRST
   EXIT(0)

DISPDOC:
   ADDRESS TSO "CLEAR"
   SAY "SQUSH - LEFT JUSTIFY AND REMOVE EXTRA BLANKS              "
   SAY
   SAY " FORMAT "
   SAY
   SAY "    SQUSH  ( LEFT-COLUMN  RIGHT-COLUMN )                  "
   SAY
   SAY "       PROCESS ENTIRE FILE OR C/CC/C# DELIMITED RANGE AND "
   SAY "       LEFT JUSTIFY AND SQUEEZE OUT EXTRA BLANKS. EITHER  "
   SAY "       THE SPECIFIED COLUMNS OR THE CURRENT BOUNDS ARE    "
   SAY "       USED TO LIMIT PROCESSING.                          "
   SAY
   EXIT(1)

./       ADD   NAME=SUBCAN
/* REXX - SUBCAN: EDIT MACRO TO SUBMIT JCL AND CANCEL CHANGES         */
/**********************************************************************/

   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "ISREDIT MACRO (PARMS)"
   IF SUBSTR(PARMS,1,1) = '?' THEN SIGNAL DISPDOC

   ADDRESS ISREDIT "SUBMIT"
   ADDRESS ISREDIT "CANCEL"

   EXIT 0

DISPDOC:
   ADDRESS TSO "CLEAR"
   SAY "SUBCAN -- SUBMIT JOB AND CANCEL EDIT SESSION           "
   SAY
   SAY "  SUBCAN  ( ? )                                        "
   SAY
   SAY "  SIMPLY SUBMITS THE EDITED FILE AND DOES A CANCEL.    "
   SAY "  THE ONLY PARAMETER, A QUESTION MARK (?), CAUSES      "
   SAY "  THIS VERY MINIMAL HELP TO BE DISPLAYED.              "
   SAY
   EXIT(1)
./       ADD   NAME=SUBO
/**  REXX  --  SUBMIT THE JOB AFTER SUBSTITUTIONS  **/

   SAVEMSG = MSG("OFF")
   SUBCOM ISPEXEC
   IF RC <> 0 THEN DO
      SAY 'SUBO MUST BE RUN UNDER ISPF!'
      SIGNAL EOJ
   END
   SUBCOM ISREDIT
   IF RC = 0 THEN DO
      ADDRESS ISPEXEC "CONTROL ERRORS RETURN"
      ADDRESS ISREDIT,
         "ISREDIT MACRO (PARMS) PROCESS"
      IF RC = 0 THEN DO
         ADDRESS ISREDIT "ISREDIT ("DSN") = DATASET"
      END
   END
   IF DSN = 'DSN' THEN DO
      ARG PARMS
      SIGNAL DSLIST
   END

   IF SUBSTR(PARMS,1,1) = '?' THEN SIGNAL DISPDOC
   CALL PARSE_PARMS
   "ISREDIT (THISMEM) = MEMBER"
   "ISREDIT (THISDSN) = DATASET"
   IF THISMEM <> ""
      THEN ZINPDSN = "'" || THISDSN || "(" || THISMEM || ")'"
      ELSE ZINPDSN = "'" || THISDSN || "'"

   ADDRESS TSO
   "FREE DD(SUBODD)"
   "ALLOC DD(SUBODD) SYSOUT(A) WRITER(INTRDR)"
   "EXECIO 0 DISKW "SUBODD"(OPEN"
   "ISREDIT (START) = LINENUM" .ZFIRST
   "ISREDIT (END)   = LINENUM" .ZLAST

   ORIGIN_NOW = "YES"
   DO PNTR =  START  TO  END  BY  1
      "ISREDIT (RECORD)   = LINE &PNTR"
      AMPER = 0
      XX = INDEX(RECORD,"&")
      IF XX > 0 THEN DO WHILE XX > 0
         CALL PROCESS_TOKENS
      END
      IF AMPER > 0 THEN DO KK = 1 TO AMPER
         LL = REAL.KK
         RECORD = OVERLAY('&',RECORD,LL,1)
      END
      QUEUE RECORD
      "EXECIO 1 DISKW" SUBODD
      IF ORIGIN = "YES" THEN DO
         IF ORIGIN_NOW = "YES" THEN DO
            DO II = 71 TO 1 BY -1 WHILE SUBSTR(RECORD,II,1) = " "
            END
            IF SUBSTR(RECORD,II,1) <> "," THEN DO
               CALL GEN_ORIGIN
               ORIGIN_NOW = "NO"
            END
         END
      END
   END

   IF ABEND <> "NO" THEN CALL GEN_ABEND
   "EXECIO 0 DISKW "SUBODD"(FINIS"
   "FREE DD(SUBODD)"
   CALL SETMSG "* NO JOB SUBMITTED$JOB SUBMITTED SUCCESSFULLY!"
   EXIT(0)

DSLIST:
   DO II = LENGTH(PARMS)-1 TO 1 BY -1 WHILE(SUBSTR(PARMS,II,1) <> "'")
   END II
   ZINPDSN = SUBSTR(PARMS,II)
   PARMS   = SUBSTR(PARMS,1,II-1)

   CALL PARSE_PARMS

   ADDRESS TSO
   "FREE DD(DDXX SUBODD)"
   "ALLOC DSN("ZINPDSN") DD(DDXX) SHR"
   "ALLOC DD(SUBODD) SYSOUT(A) WRITER(INTRDR)"
   "EXECIO 0 DISKR" DDXX   "(OPEN"
   "EXECIO 0 DISKW" SUBODD "(OPEN"

   "EXECIO 1 DISKR" DDXX
   RET_CD     = RC
   ORIGIN_NOW = 'YES'
   DO WHILE ( RET_CD = 0 )
      PULL RECORD
      AMPER = 0
      XX = INDEX(RECORD,"&")
      IF XX > 0 THEN DO WHILE XX > 0
         CALL PROCESS_TOKENS
      END
      IF AMPER > 0 THEN DO KK = 1 TO AMPER
         LL = REAL.KK
         RECORD = OVERLAY('&',RECORD,LL,1)
      END
      QUEUE RECORD
      "EXECIO 1 DISKW" SUBODD
      IF ORIGIN = 'YES' THEN DO
         IF ORIGIN_NOW = 'YES' THEN DO
            DO II = 71 TO 1 BY -1 WHILE SUBSTR(RECORD,II,1) = ' '
            END
            IF SUBSTR(RECORD,II,1) <> ',' THEN DO
               CALL GEN_ORIGIN
               ORIGIN_NOW = 'NO'
            END
         END
      END
      "EXECIO 1 DISKR" DDXX
      RET_CD = RC
   END

   IF ABEND <> "NO" THEN CALL GEN_ABEND

   "EXECIO 0 DISKW" DDXX "(FINIS"
   "FREE DD(DDXX SUBDDX)"
   EXIT(0)

PROCESS_TOKENS:
   IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,10) = "CCYY/MM/DD" THEN DO
      SS = DATE(S)
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || SUBSTR(SS,1,4) || "/" || SUBSTR(SS,5,2),
         || "/" || SUBSTR(SS,7,2),
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+11)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,08) = "CCYY/DDD" THEN DO
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || LEFT(DATE(S),4) || "/" || RIGHT(DATE(J),3),
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+9)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,07) = "CCYYDDD" THEN DO
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || LEFT(DATE(S),4) || RIGHT(DATE(J),3),
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+8)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,08) = "CCYYMMDD" THEN DO
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || DATE(S),
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+9)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,08) = "DD/MM/YY" THEN DO
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || DATE(E),
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+9)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,08) = "HH:MM:SS" THEN DO
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || TIME(),
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+9)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,05) = "HH:MM" THEN DO
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || LEFT(TIME(),5),
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+6)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,06) = "HHMMSS" THEN DO
      SS = TIME()
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || SUBSTR(SS,1,2),
         || SUBSTR(SS,4,2),
         || SUBSTR(SS,7,2),
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+7)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,04) = "HHMM"  THEN DO
      SS = TIME()
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || SUBSTR(SS,1,2),
         || SUBSTR(SS,4,2),
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+5)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,08) = "MM/DD/YY" THEN DO
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || DATE(U),
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+9)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,06) = "MMDDYY" THEN DO
      SS = DATE(U)
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || SUBSTR(SS,1,2),
         || SUBSTR(SS,4,2),
         || SUBSTR(SS,7,2),
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+7)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,05) = "MONTH" THEN DO
      SS = DATE(U)
      II = SUBSTR(SS,1,2)
      IF II = 1 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'JANUARY'
         ELSE IF II =  2 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'FEBRUARY'
         ELSE IF II =  3 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'MARCH'
         ELSE IF II =  4 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'APRIL'
         ELSE IF II =  5 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'MAY'
         ELSE IF II =  6 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'JUNE'
         ELSE IF II =  7 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'JULY'
         ELSE IF II =  8 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'AUGUST'
         ELSE IF II =  9 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'SEPTEMBER'
         ELSE IF II = 10 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'OCTOBER'
         ELSE IF II = 11 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'NOVEMBER'
         ELSE IF II = 12 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'DECEMBER'
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || MONTH_NAME,
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+6)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,03) = "MON" THEN DO
      SS = DATE(U)
      II = SUBSTR(SS,1,2)
      IF II = 1 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'JAN'
         ELSE IF II =  2 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'FEB'
         ELSE IF II =  3 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'MAR'
         ELSE IF II =  4 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'APR'
         ELSE IF II =  5 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'MAY'
         ELSE IF II =  6 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'JUN'
         ELSE IF II =  7 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'JUL'
         ELSE IF II =  8 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'AUG'
         ELSE IF II =  9 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'SEP'
         ELSE IF II = 10 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'OCT'
         ELSE IF II = 11 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'NOV'
         ELSE IF II = 12 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'DEC'
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || MONTH_NAME,
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+4)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,07) = "DAYOFWK" THEN DO
      II = DATE('B')//7
      IF II = 0 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'MONDAY'
         ELSE IF II =  1 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'TUESDAY'
         ELSE IF II =  2 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'WEDNESDAY'
         ELSE IF II =  3 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'THURSDAY'
         ELSE IF II =  4 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'FRIDAY'
         ELSE IF II =  5 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'SATURDAY'
         ELSE IF II =  6 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'SUNDAY'
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || MONTH_NAME,
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+8)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,03) = "DOW" THEN DO
      II = DATE('B')//7
      IF II = 0 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'MON'
         ELSE IF II =  1 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'TUE'
         ELSE IF II =  2 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'WED'
         ELSE IF II =  3 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'THU'
         ELSE IF II =  4 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'FRI'
         ELSE IF II =  5 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'SAT'
         ELSE IF II =  6 THEN MONTH_NAME = 'SUN'
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || MONTH_NAME,
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+4)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,06) = "USERID" THEN DO
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || USERID(),
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+7)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,04) = "YEAR" THEN DO
      SS = DATE(S)
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || SUBSTR(SS,1,4),
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+5)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,08) = "YY/MM/DD" THEN DO
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || DATE(O),
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+9)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,05) = "YYDDD" THEN DO
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || DATE(J),
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+6)
   END
   ELSE IF SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+1,06) = "YYMMDD" THEN DO
      SS = DATE(U)
      RECORD = SUBSTR(RECORD,1,XX-1),
         || SUBSTR(SS,7,2),
         || SUBSTR(SS,1,2),
         || SUBSTR(SS,4,2),
         || SUBSTR(RECORD,XX+7)
   END
   ELSE DO
      RECORD = OVERLAY('.',RECORD,XX,1)
      AMPER = AMPER + 1
      REAL.AMPER = XX
   END
   XX = INDEX(RECORD,"&")
   RETURN

SETMSG:
   PARSE ARG ZERRHM ZERRALRM ZERRSM'$'ZERRLM
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC 'SETMSG MSG(ISRZ002) COND'
   RETURN

GEN_ORIGIN:
   ORGREC = "//***"
   QUEUE ORGREC
   "EXECIO 1 DISKW" SUBODD
   DD = SUBSTR(DATE(U),4,2)
   IF SUBSTR(DD,2,1) = '1'         THEN XX = 'ST'
      ELSE IF SUBSTR(DD,2,1) = '2' THEN XX = 'ND'
      ELSE IF SUBSTR(DD,2,1) = '3' THEN XX = 'RD'
      ELSE XX = 'TH'
   IF SUBSTR(DD,1,1) = '0'         THEN DD = SUBSTR(DD,2)
   UDOW = TRANSLATE(DATE(W))
   UMON = TRANSLATE(DATE(M))
   ORGREC = "//***  SUBMITTED BY ",
      || USERID() || " ON " || UDOW || " " || UMON,
      || " " || DD||XX',' SUBSTR(DATE(S),1,4),
      || " (DAY" SUBSTR(DATE(J),3,3)")"
   QUEUE ORGREC
   "EXECIO 1 DISKW" SUBODD
   ORGREC = "//***    " || " AT " || TIME(),
      ||  " FROM " || ZINPDSN
   QUEUE ORGREC
   "EXECIO 1 DISKW" SUBODD
   ORGREC = "//***"
   QUEUE ORGREC
   "EXECIO 1 DISKW" SUBODD
   ORIGIN = "NO"
   RETURN

PARSE_PARMS:
   PARMS     = TRANSLATE(PARMS)
   ABEND     = "NO"
   CODE      = "666"
   ORIGIN    = "YES"
   DO II = 1 TO 10
      TOKEN = WORD(PARMS,II)
      IF TOKEN = "" THEN LEAVE
      IF TOKEN = "ORIGIN" | TOKEN = "ORG" | TOKEN = "O",
         THEN ORIGIN = "YES"
      IF SUBSTR(TOKEN,1,5) = "ABEND" THEN DO
         IF LENGTH(TOKEN) = 5 THEN ABEND = "0,LT"
         ELSE ABEND = SUBSTR(TOKEN,7,LENGTH(TOKEN)-7)
      END
      IF SUBSTR(TOKEN,1,4) = "CODE" THEN DO
         CODE = SUBSTR(TOKEN,6,LENGTH(TOKEN)-6)
      END
   END II
   RETURN

GEN_ABEND:
   ABENDREC = "//***"
   QUEUE ABENDREC
   "EXECIO 1 DISKW" SUBODD
   ABENDREC = "//ABEND      EXEC",
      || "     PGM=ABENDX,PARM=",
      || CODE || ",COND=(" || ABEND || ")"
   QUEUE ABENDREC
   "EXECIO 1 DISKW" SUBODD
   ABENDREC = "//STEPLIB      DD       DISP=SHR,DSN=",
      || "-YOUR-LOADLIB-"
   QUEUE ABENDREC
   "EXECIO 1 DISKW" SUBODD
   ABENDREC = "//***"
   QUEUE ABENDREC
   "EXECIO 1 DISKW" SUBODD
   RETURN

DISPDOC:
   ADDRESS TSO "CLEAR"
   SAY "SUBO -- SUBMIT FILE WITH VAR'S SUB & ORIGIN & ABEND   "
   SAY
   SAY "   SUBO  ( ABEND(COND) )  ( CODE(#) )  ( NOORIGIN )   "
   SAY
   SAY "     ABEND SPECIFIES COND CODE, DEFAULTS TO '0,LT';   "
   SAY "     CODE SPECIFIES USER ABEND CODE, DEFAULTS TO 666; "
   SAY "     NOORIGIN CAUSES COMMENTS WITH DATE/TIME, SOURCE  "
   SAY "     AND USER NOT TO BE DISPLAYED. TOKENS ARE:        "
   SAY
   SAY "       &CCYY/MM/DD ==> 2001/02/03                     "
   SAY "       &CCYY/DDD   ==> 2001/034                       "
   SAY "       &CCYYDDD    ==> 2001034                        "
   SAY "       &CCYYMMDD   ==> 20010203                       "
   SAY "       &DAYOFWK    ==> SATURDAY                       "
   SAY "       &DD/MM/YY   ==> 03/02/01                       "
   SAY "       &DOW        ==> SAT                            "
   SAY "       &HH:MM      ==> 12:34                          "
   SAY "       &HH:MM:SS   ==> 12:34:56                       "
   SAY "       &HHMM       ==> 1234                           "
   SAY "       &HHMMSS     ==> 123456                         "
   SAY "       &MM/DD/YY   ==> 02/03/01                       "
   SAY "       &MMDDYY     ==> 020301                         "
   SAY "       &MON        ==> FEB                            "
   SAY "       &MONTH      ==> FEBRUARY                       "
   SAY "       &USERID     ==> SPRK0JG                        "
   SAY "       &YY/MM/DD   ==> 01/02/03                       "
   SAY "       &YYDDD      ==> 01034                          "
   SAY "       &YYMMDD     ==> 010203                         "
   SAY
   EXIT(1)
./       ADD   NAME=SUFFLINE
/**  REXX -- SUFF -- WILL SUFFIX LINES WITH A CHARACTER STRING  **/
   ADDRESS ISREDIT "MACRO (PARM1) NOPROCESS"
   IF RC > 0 THEN DO
      SIGNAL NOT_IN_EDIT
      SAY "THIS IS AN EDIT MACRO"
      EXIT
   END

   IF PARM1 = "" | PARM1 = "?"  THEN SIGNAL DISPDOC

   ADDRESS ISREDIT "(TYPE) = PROFILE"

   PARM1 = TRANSLATE(PARM1)
   IF PARM1 = "QUOTE"       THEN PARM1 = '"'
   IF PARM1 = "APOSTROPHE"  THEN PARM1 = "'"
   IF PARM1 = "APOST"       THEN PARM1 = "'"
   IF PARM1 = "COMMA"       THEN PARM1 = ","

   ADDRESS ISPEXEC
   'CONTROL ERRORS RETURN'
   'ISREDIT PROCESS RANGE C  '
   SELECT
      WHEN RC = 0 THEN DO
         'ISREDIT (CMD) = RANGE_CMD'
         'ISREDIT (LINE1) = LINENUM .ZFRANGE'
         'ISREDIT (LINE2) = LINENUM .ZLRANGE'
         LINESTOCUT = LINE2 - LINE1 + 1
      END
      WHEN RC <= 4 THEN DO                      /* NO C OR M ENTERED */
         'ISREDIT (LINE1) = LINENUM .ZFRANGE'
         'ISREDIT (LINE2) = LINENUM .ZLRANGE'
         LINESTOCUT = LINE2 - LINE1 + 1
      END
      OTHERWISE  /* LINE COMMAND CONFLICT - EDIT WILL CREATE MESSAGE */
          EXIT 12
   END  /* SELECT */

/* PUT THE LINES IN STEM VARBLE */
   CUTCNT = 0  /* CHANGE LATER */
   DO I = LINE1 TO LINE2
      CUTCNT = CUTCNT + 1
      'ISREDIT (CL'CUTCNT') = LINE' I
      'ISREDIT (CURLINE) = LINE' I
      NEWLINE = CURLINE
      IF NEWLINE = COPIES(" ",LENGTH(NEWLINE)) THEN DO
         NEWLENGTH = LENGTH(NEWLINE) - LENGTH(PARM1)
      END
      ELSE DO
         NEWLINE = REVERSE(NEWLINE)
         PARM1R  = REVERSE(PARM1)
         DO I2 = 1 TO LENGTH(NEWLINE)
            IF SUBSTR(NEWLINE,I2,1) <> " " THEN DO
               NEWLINE = COPIES(" ",I2-1)""PARM1R""SUBSTR(NEWLINE,I2)
               LEAVE I2
            END
         END I2
      NEWLINE = REVERSE(NEWLINE)
      END
      "ISREDIT LINE" I "= (NEWLINE)"
      CL.0 = CUTCNT
   END I
   EXIT(0)

BAD_INPUT:
   ZEDSMSG = "PARM MISSING"
   ZEDLMSG = "RE-EXECUTE FROM COMMAND LINE: SUFF CHARACTER-TO-SUFFIX"
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "SETMSG MSG(ISRZ001)"
   EXIT(1)

NOT_IN_EDIT:
   ZEDSMSG = "NOT IN ISPF EDIT"
   ZEDLMSG = "THIS MUST BE EXECUTED WHILE IN ISPF EDIT AS A MACRO. "
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "SETMSG MSG(ISRZ001)"
   EXIT(1)

DISPDOC:
   ADDRESS TSO "CLEAR"
   SAY "                                                             "
   SAY "  SUFFLINE  APPENDS A STRING TO THE END OF EVERY SELECTED    "
   SAY "            LINE (VIA C/CC/C#) OR TO EVERY LINE IN THE FILE. "
   SAY "                                                             "
   SAY "     IF YOU WANT TO SUFFIX WITH A QUOTE, USE THE WORD        "
   SAY "     QUOTE; IF YOU WANT TO SUFFIX WITH AN APOSTROPHE,        "
   SAY "     USE THE WORD APOST; IF YOU WANT TO SUFFIX WITH A        "
   SAY "     COMMA, USE THE WORD COMMA.                              "
   SAY
   SAY "     FOR EXAMPLE,                                            "
   SAY "        SUFFLINE |                                           "
   SAY "     WILL APPEND A VERTICAL BAR TO THE END OF EACH LINE.     "
   SAY
   EXIT(1)

./       ADD   NAME=SUMCOLS
/**  REXX -- SUMS SPECIFIED COLUMNS  **/
   Numeric Digits 31
   Address "ISREDIT";
   "MACRO (PRM1 PRM2 PRM3 PRM4 PRM5 PRM6 PRM7 PRM8 PRM9 PRM10",
          "PRM11 PRM12 PRM13 PRM14 PRM15 PRM16 PRM17 PRM18 PRM19",
          "PRM20) NOPROCESS"
   If PRM1 = '' | PRM1 = '?' then signal DISPDOC

   Labels = 0
   Pairs  = 0
   tok.   = ""
   Do I = 1 to 20
      x = value("PRM"I)
      If x = "" then I = 20
      Else do
         If substr(x,1,1) = '.' then do
            If Labels = 0 then LabFrom = x
            Else LabTo = x
            Labels = Labels + 1
         End
         Else do
            Pairs = Pairs + 1
            tok.i = value("PRM"I)
            If  ¬DATATYPE(tok.i,"N")  then do
               ZEDSMSG = 'Bad Column'
               ZEDLMSG = "Columns must be numeric," tok.i "is not"
               Address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISRZ000)"
               Exit(4)
            End
         End
      End
   End  /* Do I = 1 to 20 */

   If Labels > 0 & Labels <> 2 then do
      ZEDSMSG = "Too many lbls"
      ZEDLMSG = Labels "is too many labels"
      Address "ISPEXEC" "SETMSG MSG(ISRZ000)"
      Exit(4)
   End
   If Labels = 2 then do
      "(LineBgn) = LINENUM " LabFrom
      "(LineEnd) = LINENUM " LabTo
   End
   Else do
      "PROCESS RANGE C"
      rch = RC
      If rch = 0 then do
         "(ZFRANGE) = LINENUM .ZFRANGE"
         "(ZLRANGE) = LINENUM .ZLRANGE"
         Labels = 2
      End
      Else do
         If rch =  4  then do
            "(ZFRANGE) = LINENUM .ZFIRST"
            "(ZLRANGE) = LINENUM .ZLAST"
            Labels = 2
         End
         Else do
            "LINE_BEFORE .ZFIRST = NOTELINE ",
             "'ISREDIT PROCESS C or RANGE CC return code is" rch"'"
             Exit(4)
         End
      End
      LineBgn = ZFRANGE
      LineEnd = ZLRANGE
   End

   If LineEnd < LineBgn then do
      x = LineBgn
      LineBgn = LineEnd
      LineEnd = x
   End
   IF LineBgn = 0 THEN LineBgn = 1
   sum. = 0

   Do I = LineBgn to LineEnd by 1
      "(XLINE)   = LINE" I
      "(XSTATUS) = XSTATUS" I
      If xstatus = "NX" then do
         Rowtot = 0
         Do J = 1 to 17 by 2
            If tok.J = "" then leave
            jp1 = J + 1
            bb = tok.jp1 - tok.J + 1
            addend = substr(XLINE,tok.J,bb)
            ii = index(addend,',')
            Do while ii <> 0
               addend = substr(addend,1,ii-1),
                  || substr(addend,ii+1)
               ii = index(addend,',')
            End
            If addend <> ' ' then do
               If index(addend,'+') = 0 & index(addend,'-') = 0 then do
                  Do ii = length(addend) to 1 by -1,
                     while ( substr(addend,ii,1) = ' ' )
                  End
                  kk = substr(addend,ii,1)
                  If kk < '0' | kk > '9' then do
                     kk = translate(kk)
                     If verify(kk,'}JKLMNOPQR') = 0
                        then addend = '-' || substr(addend,1,ii-1),
                           || translate(kk,'0123456789','}JKLMNOPQR')
                     Else if verify(kk,'{ABCDEFGHI') = 0
                        then addend = '+' || substr(addend,1,ii-1),
                           || translate(kk,'0123456789','{ABCDEFGHI')
                  End
               End
               Else do
                  If index(addend,'+') <> 0 then do
                     ii = index(addend,'+')
                     addend = '+' || substr(addend,1,ii-1),
                        || substr(addend,ii+1)
                  End
                  Else do
                     ii = index(addend,'-')
                     addend = '-' || substr(addend,1,ii-1),
                        || substr(addend,ii+1)
                  End
               End
            End
            If  DATATYPE(addend,"N")  then do
               sum.J  = sum.J  + addend
               Rowtot = Rowtot + addend
            End
         End  /* Do J = 1 to 19 by 2 */
      End
   End  /* Do I = LineBgn to LineEnd by 1 */

   sumtot = 0;
   "(LASTLN) = LINENUM .zlast"
   If lastln \= LineEnd then LineEnd = LineEnd + 1
   Tallies = 1
   Do J=1 to 17 by  2
      jp1 = J + 1
      If tok.J <> "" then do
         Tallies = Tallies + 1
         sumtot = sumtot + sum.J
         "LINE_BEFORE" LineBgn "= NOTELINE """||TIME('N') ,
         "SUM of COLS " tok.J||"-"||tok.jp1||", total is" sum.J""""
      End
   End
   "LINE_BEFORE" LineBgn "= NOTELINE '"||TIME('N'),
          "--------------- Total of SUMS is " sumtot "'"
   "Loc " LineBgn
   "Up " Tallies
   Exit(0)

DISPDOC:
   ADDRESS TSO "CLEAR"
   SAY "SUMCOLS - Add columns of numbers under Edit/View "
   SAY
   SAY " Format "
   SAY "    SUMCOLS  1st-col 2nd-col  ( ... )  ( .A .B )        "
   SAY "       At least one set of columns is mandatory. Up to  "
   SAY "       10 sets may be supplied.  Either a CC/CC range   "
   SAY "       may be delimited, labels may be supplied, or the "
   SAY "       whole file will be processed.  The data may be   "
   SAY "       staggered, have decimal places, and/or be signed."
   SAY
   SAY " Example "
   SAY "            1---5---10----5---20---                 "
   SAY "              1        -1.1                         "
   SAY "              3            1.1                      "
   SAY "              5          2.3                        "
   SAY "    Given the above data, SUMCOLS  1 5  11 20       "
   SAY "    will produce                                    "
   SAY "       SUM of NX COLS  1-5, total is 9              "
   SAY "       SUM of NX COLS  11-20, total is 2.3          "
   SAY "       --------------- Total of SUMS is  11.3       "
   SAY
   Exit(1)

./       ADD   NAME=VC
  /* REXX */                                                            00000200
  /*         EXEC SEARCHES PROD.COPYLIB AND PRBT.COPYLIB AND      */    00000300

  SAY 'PRESENT IN PROD.COPYLIB'                                         00001400

./       ADD   NAME=VINF
   /* REXX */                                                           00000100
      ADDRESS ISREDIT "MACRO NOPROCESS (VIN)"                           00000210
      IF LENGTH(VIN) ¬= 17 THEN  DO                                     00000300
         ZEDSMSG = INVALID VIN# !!                                      00000400

      "(LINE,COL) = CURSOR"                                             00000900
                                                                        00001000
      IF LINE = 1  THEN DO
          LINE = 0
      END
                                                                        00001000
      F1 = "  AND V6_SERIAL       =  "                                  00002000
      F2 = F1 || "'" || F || "'"                                        00002100
      "LINE_AFTER (LINE) = (F2)"                                        00002200

      "LINE_AFTER (LINE) = (E2)"                                        00002330

      V6 = "  AND V6_YEAR         =  "                                  00002350

      C2 = C1 || "'" || C || "'"                                        00002391
      "LINE_AFTER (LINE) = (C2)"                                        00002392
                                                                        00002393
      B1 = "  AND V6_VDS          = "                                   00002394
      B2 = B1 || "'" || B || "'"                                        00002395
      "LINE_AFTER (LINE) = (B2)"                                        00002396
                                                                        00002397

./       ADD   NAME=VSAVE
/** REXX - SAVE command for VIEW **************************************/
/*                                                                    */
/* Provides the equivalent of the SAVE command in a View session.     */
/* It uses REPLACE to write the data and LMMSTATS to set the          */
/* statistics.                                                        */
/*                                                                    */
/**********************************************************************/
   ADDRESS 'ISPEXEC'
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "ISREDIT MACRO (PARMS)"
   IF SUBSTR(PARMS,1,1) = '?' THEN SIGNAL DISPDOC
   IF RC > 0 THEN EXIT RC /* not an EDIT macro */
   "CONTROL ERRORS RETURN"
   "ISREDIT (zdsn) = DATASET"
   "ISREDIT (zmemb) = MEMBER"
   IF ZMEMB='' THEN CALL PROCESS_SEQUENTIAL_DATA_SET
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
/*     Fast-path processing when STATS=OFF                          */
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
   "ISREDIT (stats) = STATS"
   IF STATS='OFF' THEN DO
      "ISREDIT REPLACE" ZMEMB ".ZFIRST .ZLAST"
      CALL CHECK_RC RC,0,'REPLACE'
      "SETMSG MSG(ISRE016)"
      EXIT
   END
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
/*     Prevent LMMSTATS failure when VERSION=00                     */
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
   "ISREDIT (zlvers) = VERSION"
   IF ZLVERS = 0 THEN DO
      ZEDSMSG = "Invalid Version"
      ZEDLMSG = "Version 00 is not supported by the LMMSTATS service".
         "SETMSG MSG(ISRZ001)"
      EXIT 4             /* not supported in this release */
   END
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
/*     Retrieve current statistics from member's directory entry    */
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
   "ISREDIT (dataid) = DATAID"
   "LMOPEN DATAID("DATAID")"
   CALL CHECK_RC RC,0,'LMOPEN'
   "LMMFIND DATAID("DATAID") MEMBER("ZMEMB") STATS(YES)"
   LMMFIND_RC=RC
   CALL CHECK_RC RC,8,'LMMFIND'
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
/*     Rewrite member using the REPLACE command                     */
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
   "ISREDIT (n1,n2) = NUMBER"
   MODLINES=0 /* modified lines  */
   IF N1='ON' & LEFT(N2,1)='S' THEN DO  /* NUMBER ON STD   */
      "ISREDIT (ustat) = USER_STATE" /* push user_state */
      CALL COUNT_MODLINES /* Cound modified lines   */
      "ISREDIT REPLACE" ZMEMB ".ZF .ZL"
      XRC = RC
      "ISREDIT USER_STATE = (ustat)" /* pop user_state  */
      CALL CHECK_RC XRC,0,'REPLACE'
   END
   ELSE DO /* NUMBER OFF      */
      "ISREDIT REPLACE" ZMEMB ".ZF .ZL"
      CALL CHECK_RC RC,0,'REPLACE'
   END
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
/*     Update statistics using LMMSTATS                             */
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
   "ISREDIT (zlvers) = VERSION" /* NEW VERSION   */
   "ISREDIT (zlmod) = LEVEL" /* NEW LEVEL     */
   IF LMMFIND_RC=8 THEN /* new member    */
      "LMMSTATS DATAID("DATAID") MEMBER("ZMEMB")" "VERSION("ZLVERS") ,
      MODLEVEL("ZLMOD")" "MODRECS("MODLINES+0")"
   ELSE /* member existed before */
      "LMMSTATS DATAID("DATAID") MEMBER("ZMEMB")" "VERSION("ZLVERS") ,
      MODLEVEL("ZLMOD")" "CREATED("ZLCDATE") INITSIZE("ZLINORC")" ,
      "MODRECS("MODLINES+0")"
   CALL CHECK_RC RC,0,'LMMSTATS'
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
/*     Issue completion message and exit                            */
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
   "LMCLOSE DATAID("DATAID")"
   CALL CHECK_RC RC,0,'LMCLOSE'
   "SETMSG MSG(ISRE016)" /* member zmemb saved */
   EXIT
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
/*     Count_modlines internal function: Count modified lines       */
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
COUNT_MODLINES:
   "ISREDIT NUMBER OFF"
   "ISREDIT (recfm) = RECFM"
   IF RECFM='F' THEN
      "ISREDIT (lrecl) = LRECL"
   ELSE
      LRECL=8 /* RECFM=V        */
   "ISREDIT (modlines) = LINENUM .ZL" /* total number of lines*/
   "ISREDIT SEEK '00' ALL" LRECL-1 /*count unmodified lines*/
   IF RC=0 THEN
      DO
         "ISREDIT (c1,c2) = SEEK_COUNTS"
         MODLINES=MODLINES-C1 /* modified lines*/
      END
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
/*           Process a sequential data set                          */
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
PROCESS_SEQUENTIAL_DATA_SET:
   "ISREDIT REPLACE '"zdsn"'" .zfirst .zlast
   "SETMSG MSG(ISRE016)"
   EXIT
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
/*           Error routine                                          */
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
CHECK_RC:
   IF ARG(1) \> ARG(2) THEN RETURN /* RC=0 */
   "SETMSG MSG("ZERRMSG")"
   "LMCLOSE DATAID("DATAID")"
   EXIT 20
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
/*           Built-in Help                                          */
/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
DISPDOC:
   ADDRESS TSO "CLEAR"
   SAY "VSAVE -- SAVES FILE/MEMBER FROM WITHIN VIEW            "
   SAY
   SAY "  VSAVE   ( ? )                                        "
   SAY
   SAY "  WILL SAVE EITHER A VIEWED MEMBER OR SEQUENTIAL FILE, "
   SAY "  WITHOUT HAVING TO DO A MANUAL REPLACE. THE ONLY      "
   SAY "  PARAMETER, A QUESTION MARK (?), CAUSES THIS VERY     "
   SAY "  MINIMAL HELP TO BE DISPLAYED.                        "
   SAY
   EXIT(1)
./       ADD   NAME=VW
/**  REXX -- VIEW  **/
   ZEDLMSG = ""
   RSLT = ""
   SAVEMSG = MSG()
   if SAVEMSG = 'ON'  then  X = MSG("OFF")
   MSGTYPE = "ISRZ001"
   X = ADDRESS()
   SUBCOM ISREDIT
   if RC <> 0  then do
        UMODE = "NATIVE"
        ARG FNAME VOLSER
        SETMSG = "     Must be run under ISPF"
        call SETM
        RSLT = " NOT in ISPF - UNABLE to run."
        signal BYEBYE
   end
   address ISPEXEC "CONTROL ERRORS RETURN"
   address ISREDIT "ISREDIT MACRO ("FNAME","VOLSER")"
   if RC <> 0  then do
        UMODE = "ISPEXEC"
        ARG FNAME VOLSER
   end
   else  do
      UMODE = "ISREDIT"
      address ISREDIT "ISREDIT ("LIN","COL") = CURSOR"
   end

CHKDSN:
   WFILE = ""
   if FNAME = ""  then do
      SETMSG = "     You must supply the DSN to VIEW.",
         "  I.E. VIEW 'some.filename'"
      call SETM
      RSLT = "NO DSN SUPPLIED"
      signal BYEBYE
   end
   if substr(FNAME,1,1)="'" & substr(FNAME,length(FNAME),1)="'" then do
      LEN = length(FNAME)-2
      WFILE = substr(FNAME,2,LEN)
      signal BROWSIT
   end
   call UPROFREX
   PROFILE = RESULT
   if index(PROFILE,'NOPREFIX') = 0    then  WFILE = USERID()"."FNAME
   else WFILE = FNAME

BROWSIT:
   upper WFILE
   if VOLSER = ""  &  sysdsn(''''WFILE'''') <> 'OK'  then do
      SETMSG= "     Can't find "WFILE". It may not be CATALOGED or",
              "you didn't spell the file correctly, or you didn't use",
              "QUOTES if they were required, or file may be HELD by ",
              "another task."
      call SETM
      RSLT = "NOT FOUND"
      signal BYEBYE
   end
   if VOLSER = "" then Address ISPEXEC "SELECT PGM(ISPSTRT)",
      "PARM(CMD(ISREPDF '"WFILE"' V))"
   else address ISPEXEC "VIEW DATASET('"WFILE"') VOLUME("VOLSER")"
   BRC = RC
   if BRC = 0  then do
      RSLT = "FOUND"
      signal OKVIEW
   end

   X = VSAMCHK(WFILE)
   if X = 1  then do
      SETMSG = "     "WFILE" is a VSAM file. Cannot VIEW it."
      call SETM
      RSLT = "NO ACTION-VSAM FILE"
      signal BYEBYE
   end

   VOLS = GVOLS(WFILE)
   VOLCNT = words(VOLS)
   if VOLCNT = 1  then do
      if VOLSER <> "" then VOLDATA = "VOLUME("VOLSER")"
      else VOLDATA = ""
      D=LISTDSI((FNAME) VOLDATA 'NODIRECTORY')
      if D <> 0  then do
         SETMSG = "     "WFILE", VOL "VOLDATA" LISTDSI error. RC=",
                 D". "SYSMSGLVL2
         call SETM
         RSLT = "LISTDSI ERR. RC="D
         signal BYEBYE
      end
      if SYSUSED = 0  then do
         SETMSG = "     "WFILE" contains NO data. Nothing to VIEW."
         call SETM
         RSLT = "NO ACTION-EMPTY FILE"
         signal BYEBYE
      end
      if substr(SYSDSORG,1,1)<>'P' then do
         SETMSG = "     Can't VIEW "WFILE".  DSORG="SYSDSORG"."
         call SETM
         RSLT = "NO ACTION-DSORG="SYSDSORG
         signal BYEBYE
      end
   end

   VOLSER = word(VOLS,VOLCNT)

   SETMSG = "     "WFILE" was multi-volume, residing on "VOLS"."

   call SETM
   address ISPEXEC "VIEW DATASET('"WFILE"') VOLUME("VOLSER")"
   BRC = RC
   if BRC = 0  then do
      RSLT=" ON "VOLCNT" VOLS"
      signal OKVIEW
   end

   QUIT = 'N'
   do V = VOLCNT TO 1 BY -1
      if QUIT='Y' then
         NOP
      else do
         VOLSER = word(VOLS,V)
         address ISPEXEC "VIEW DATASET('"WFILE"') VOLUME("VOLSER") "
         BRC = RC
         if BRC = 0 then QUIT = "Y"
      end
   end

   if BRC = 0 then do
      RSLT = " ON "VOLCNT" VOLS-TRUNC"
      signal OKVIEW
   end

HUH:
   SETMSG = "     "WFILE" on "VOLS" cannot be VIEWED.",
            "'VIEW' RC="BRC
   call SETM
   RSLT = "NO ACTION-VIEW ERROR RC =" BRC
   signal BYEBYE

OKVIEW:
   MSGTYPE = "ISRZ000"
   signal BYEBYE

BYEBYE:
   if UMODE <> "NATIVE" then address ispexec "SETMSG MSG("MSGTYPE")"
   else say ZEDLMSG
   if SAVEMSG='ON'  then X=MSG("ON")
   EXIT  0

SETM:
   if UMODE <> "NATIVE" then
      ZEDLMSG = center(REX||VERSION,74,' ')
   else
      ZEDLMSG = center(REX||VERSION,77,' ')
   ZEDLMSG = ">"ZEDLMSG"<"
   ZEDLMSG = ZEDLMSG || SETMSG
   return
./       ADD   NAME=VWV
/** REXX -- REPRO a VSAM file to a sequential copy and View it **/
   Parse Arg Dsn
   Msg = Msg(Off)
   Dsn = Translate(Dsn)
   If substr(Dsn,1,1) = "?" | Dsn = "" then signal DISPDOC
   Parms = ''
   If words(Dsn) > 1 then do
      Do ii = length(Dsn) to 1 by -1,
            while(substr(Dsn,ii,1) <> ' ' & substr(Dsn,ii,1) <> ') ')
      End ii
      Parms = substr(Dsn,1,ii)
      Dsn   = substr(Dsn,ii+1)
   End
   'ISPEXEC CONTROL ERRORS RETURN'
   If SysDsn(Dsn) <> 'OK' then DO
       ZedSmsg=''
       'ISPEXEC SETMSG MSG(ISRZ000)'
       Exit(12)
   End
   now     = Time(s)
   Gdd     ='F'  || now
   Flat    ='FL' || now
   Vsam    ='VS' || now
   FlatDSN = '$$$TEMP.VSAM.FLAT.' || Flat
   'ALLOC DD('Vsam') DSN('Dsn') SHR REUSE'
   Call GetFileAttr
   'ALLOC F('Flat') NEW CAT REU RECFM('Recfm')',
      'LRECL('Lrecl') BLKSIZE(0)',
      'CYL SP(20 20) RELEASE DSORG(PS) DSN('FlatDSN')'
   If Rc <> 0 Then do
       Say '* ERROR allocation for' Flat 'failed with code' RC
       Exit(12)
   End
   'REPRO IFI('Vsam') OFI('Flat')' Parms
   'FREE DD('Vsam' 'Flat' ifi ofi)'
   'FREE DSN('Dsn FlatDSN')'
   ZedSmsg=''
   ZedLmsg=''
   Address ISPEXEC "SELECT PGM(ISPSTRT)",
      "PARM(CMD(ISREPDF "FlatDSN" V))"
   Exit

GetFileAttr:
   'ALLOC F('Gdd') NEW DEL REU RECFM(V B)',
      'LRECL(129) BLKSIZE(0) TR SP(5)',
       'DSORG(PS)'
   'LISTCAT ENT('Dsn') ALL OUTFILE('Gdd')'
   'EXECIO * DISKR 'Gdd' (STEM LCDATA. FINIS)'
   'FREE F('Gdd')'

   AvgLrecl = 0
   MaxLrecl = 0
   Do x = 3 to LcData.0 while(AvgLrecl = 0 | MaxLrecl = 0)
      If index(LcData.x,'AVGLRECL') <> 0 Then do
         ii = index(LcData.x,'AVGLRECL')
         do jj = (ii+8) to 125 while(substr(LcData.x,jj,1) = '-')
         end jj
         do kk = (jj+1) to 125 while(substr(LcData.x,kk,1) <> ' ')
         end kk
         AvgLrecl = substr(LcData.x,jj,kk-jj)
      End
      If index(LcData.x,'MAXLRECL') <> 0 Then do
         ii = index(LcData.x,'MAXLRECL')
         do jj = (ii+8) to 125 while(substr(LcData.x,jj,1) = '-')
         end jj
         do kk = (jj+1) to 125 while(substr(LcData.x,kk,1) <> ' ')
         end kk
         MaxLrecl = substr(LcData.x,jj,kk-jj)
      End
   End

   if AvgLrecl = MaxLrecl then do
      Recfm = 'F B'
      Lrecl = MaxLrecl
   End
   Else do
      Recfm = 'V B'
      Lrecl = MaxLrecl + 4
   End
   Return

DISPDOC:
   ADDRESS TSO "CLEAR"
   SAY "VWV  --  View all or part of a VSAM file                  "
   SAY
   SAY " FORMAT "
   SAY
   SAY "    VWV  ( limits )  VSAM-file-name                       "
   SAY
   SAY "       The VSAM file name can be specified or defaulted   "
   SAY "       from a DS List entry.  The limits must be before   "
   SAY "       the file name. They may be COUNT(#), SKIP(#),      "
   SAY "       FROMKEY(key), TOKEY(key), FROMNUMBER(#), or        "
   SAY "       TONUMBER(#). It puts you in View on the set desired"
   SAY "       but saves the time-stamped file upon exit.         "
   SAY
   SAY " EXAMPLE "
   SAY
   SAY "    VWV  COUNT(500)  A-VSAM-FILE-UNDER-YOUR-ID            "
   SAY
   SAY "       will View the first 500 records of that file and   "
   SAY "       keep the file on exiting.                          "
   SAY
   EXIT(1)

./       ADD   NAME=WHEREIS
/*************************************************************** REXX */00010000
/*                                                                    */00020000
/* Module Name = WHEREIS                                              */00030000
/*                                                                    */00040000
/* Descriptive Name = Search for a member in allocated libraries      */00050000
/*                                                                    */00060000
/* Status = R200                                                      */00070000
/*                                                                    */00080000
/* Function = Look for all occurences of a member in the libraries    */00090000
/*            currently allocated to your TSO session.                */00100000
/*            If multiple versions of the member are present in       */00110000
/*            a concatenation, they are all displayed.                */00120000
/*            ISPF stats are displayed if present.                    */00130000
/*                                                                    */00140000
/* Author   =  Gilbert Saint-flour <gsf@pobox.com>                    */00150000
/*                                                                    */00160000
/* Dependencies = TSO/E V2                                            */00170000
/*                ISPF V3 or V4                                       */00180000
/*                STEMDISP Sub-routine (optional)                     */00190000
/*                                                                    */00200000
/* SYNTAX   =  WHEREIS                                                */00210000
/*                 member                Member Name                  */00220000
/*                                                                    */00230000
/* DEFAULTS =  none                                                   */00240000
/*                                                                    */00250000
/* OPERANDS = See Below                                               */00260000
/*                                                                    */00270000
/*             member is the name of the member you are looking for.  */00280000
/*                                                                    */00290000
/* INVOCATION = WHEREIS can be invoked as a command or as an          */00300000
/*              EDIT macro.                                           */00310000
/*                                                                    */00320000
/**********************************************************************/00330000
ARG Mbr                                                                 00340000
IF Mbr='' THEN DO                      /*  IF NO ARGUMENT SPECIFIED,  */00350000
  ADDRESS ISREDIT                      /*  SWITCH TO "EDIT MACRO"     */00360000
  'MACRO (Mbr)'                        /*  MODE TO LOCATE MEMBER      */00370000
  IF RC>0 THEN EXIT RC                 /*  BEING EDITED               */00380000
  IF Mbr='' THEN DO                                                     00390000
    "(Mbr) = MEMBER"                                                    00400000
    IF RC>0 | Mbr='' THEN DO                                            00410000
      SAY 'ENTER MEMBER NAME'                                           00420000
      PULL Mbr                                                          00430000
      IF Mbr='' THEN EXIT 1            /*  User hit ENTER             */00440000
    END                                                                 00450000
  END                                                                   00460000
UPPER Mbr                                                               00470000
END                                                                     00480000
X=OUTTRAP('Hline.')                    /*  TRAP LISTALC OUTPUT        */00490000
ADDRESS TSO "LISTALC SY ST"            /*  GET DDN/DSN LIST           */00500000
X=OUTTRAP('OFF')                       /*  STOP TRAPPING              */00510000
ADDRESS ISPEXEC  ;I=0;J=0;K=1                                           00520000
                                                                        00530000
DO I=2 TO Hline.0                                                       00540000
  IF LEFT(Hline.I,2)='  ' THEN DO                                       00550000
    X=SUBSTR(Hline.I,3,8)                                               00560000
    IF LEFT(X,1)=' ' THEN                                               00570000
      J=J+1                                                             00580000
    ELSE DO;                                                            00590000
      J=0;                                                              00600000
      DDN=STRIP(X)                                                      00610000
      END                                                               00620000
    IF POS('(',Dsn)>0 THEN ITERATE                                      00630000
    IF LEFT(Dsn,1)='*' THEN ITERATE                                     00640000
    IF LEFT(Dsn,9)='TERMFILE ' THEN ITERATE                             00650000
    IF LEFT(Dsn,9)='NULLFILE ' THEN ITERATE                             00660000
    IF RIGHT(Dsn,1)='?' THEN ITERATE                                    00670000
    IF SYSDSN("'"Dsn"("Mbr")'")='OK' THEN                               00680000
      CALL GET_STATS                                                    00690000
    END                                                                 00700000
  ELSE                                                                  00710000
    Dsn=Hline.I                                                         00720000
END                                                                     00730000
                                                                        00740000
IF K>1 THEN DO                                                          00750000
  'VGET (ZENVIR)'                                                       00760000
  IF LEFT(ZENVIR,6) = 'ISPF 4' THEN                                     00770000
    Panel='ISRBROBA'                /* ISPF V4 BROWSE WITH ACTION BAR */00780000
  ELSE                                                                  00790000
    Panel='ISRBROBF'                /* ISPF V3 BROWSE (NO ACTION BAR) */00800000
  SIGNAL ON SYNTAX                /* REXXTOOLS NOT PRESENT ON SYSTEM */ 00810000
  CALL STEMDISP 'BROWSE', 'Line.',,,'Where is' Mbr,Panel                00820000
  END                                                                   00830000
EXIT                                                                    00840000
                                                                        00850000
GET_STATS:                                                              00860000
  "LMINIT DATAID(DD1) DATASET('"Dsn"') ENQ(SHR)"                        00870000
  IF RC>0 THEN SIGNAL ERROR                                             00880000
  "LMOPEN DATAID("DD1")"                                                00890000
  IF RC>0 THEN SIGNAL ERROR                                             00900000
  "LMMFIND DATAID("DD1") MEMBER("Mbr") STATS(YES)"                      00910000
  RC2=RC                                                                00920000
  "LMCLOSE DATAID("DD1")"                                               00930000
  IF RC>0 THEN SIGNAL ERROR                                             00940000
  "LMFREE DATAID("DD1")"                                                00950000
  IF RC>0 THEN SIGNAL ERROR                                             00960000
  IF RC2=0 THEN DO                                                      00970000
    X=ZLVERS'.'ZLMOD  ZLCDATE  ZLMDATE  ZLMTIME,                        00980000
      ZLCNORC ZLINORC ZLMNORC ZLUSER                                    00990000
    IF LEFT(X,1)='Z' THEN X='(NO STATS)'                                01000000
    Line.K=LEFT(DDN'+'J,12) Dsn;  L=K+1                                 01010000
    Line.L='            ' LEFT(Mbr,9) X                                 01020000
    K=K+2                                                               01030000
    END                                                                 01040000
RETURN                                                                  01050000

  END                                                                   01110000

BIG_LETTERS:                                                            01200000
  ARG STRING L                                                          01210000
  STRING=CENTER(STRING,11)                                              01220000
  DO I=L TO L+6;LINE.I=' ';END                                          01230000
  DO I=1 TO LENGTH(STRING)                                              01240000
    N=1+(INDEX(T0,TRANSLATE(SUBSTR(STRING,I,1)))-1)*5                   01250000
    P=L+1                                                               01260000
    LINE.P=LINE.P'  'SUBSTR(T1,N,5);P=P+1                               01270000
    LINE.P=LINE.P'  'SUBSTR(T2,N,5);P=P+1                               01280000
    LINE.P=LINE.P'  'SUBSTR(T3,N,5);P=P+1                               01290000
    LINE.P=LINE.P'  'SUBSTR(T4,N,5);P=P+1                               01300000
    LINE.P=LINE.P'  'SUBSTR(T5,N,5);P=P+1                               01310000
  END                                                                   01320000
  LINE.P=' '                                                            01330000
  RETURN                                                                01340000
/**********************************************************************/01350000
/*             JULIAN-TO-GREGORIAN CONVERSION ROUTINE                 */01360000
/*                   GDATE=GREGORIAN(1992134)                         */01370000
/*                      RETURNS "YYYY/MM/DD"                          */01380000
/**********************************************************************/01390000
GREGORIAN: PROCEDURE                                                    01400000
  YYYY=LEFT(ARG(1),LENGTH(ARG(1))-3)                                    01410000
  DDD=RIGHT(ARG(1),3)                                                   01420000
  T=(YYYY//4=0)                                                         01430000
  DD=DDD; IF DD>(59+T) THEN DD=DD+2-T                                   01440000
  MM=((DD+91)*100)%3055                                                 01450000
  DD=DD+91-(MM*3055)%100                                                01460000
  RETURN YYYY'/'RIGHT(MM-2,2,'0')'/'RIGHT(DD,2,'0')                     01470000
./       ADD   NAME=WHOIS
 PROC 1 USERID
 CONTROL NOMSG,NOFLUSH
 ERROR GOTO ENDIT
 CLEAR
 WRITE SEARCHING.......
 ALLOC FI(USERS) DS('JONNALR.INPUT.EPC') SH
 OPENFILE USERS INPUT
 GETMORE: -
 GETFILE USERS
 IF &USERID¬=&SUBSTR(7:14,&USERS) THEN GOTO GETMORE
 WRITE &USERID IS &SUBSTR(19:38,&USERS)
 CLOSFILE USERS
 FREE FI(USERS)
 END
 ENDIT:WRITE &USERID IS NOT KNOWN TO ME
 CLOSFILE USERS
 FREE FI(USERS)
 RETURN
 END

./       ADD   NAME=XALLMEM
/**  REXX -- Edit every member of a PDS from outside Edit  **/

   arg dsn exec
   if dsn = "?" | dsn = "" then signal DispDoc

   x = outtrap("lm.","*")
   address tso "LISTDS" dsn "MEMBERS"
   rcsave = rc
   if rcsave <> 0 then do
       say 'RC =' rcsave 'from LISTDS...'
       exit 16
   end
   x = outtrap("off")

   do i = 1 to lm.0
       if lm.i = "--MEMBERS--" then leave
   end

   do j = i+1 to lm.0
       parse value lm.j with mem extra
       if mem = exec then iterate
       if substr(dsn,1,1) = "'" | substr(dsn,1,1) = '"' then do
           dsnx = substr(dsn,2,length(dsn)-2)
           Address ISPEXEC "EDIT DATASET('"dsnx"("mem")') MACRO("exec")"
       end
       else do
           Address ISPEXEC "EDIT DATASET("dsn"("mem")) MACRO("exec")"
       end
   end

   Exit(0)

DispDoc:
   ADDRESS TSO "CLEAR"
   Say "XALLMEM -- Execute macro against all members of a PDS       "
   Say
   Say "   XALLMEM  ( ? )  PDS  Macro                               "
   Say
   Say "       PDS is the name of the Partitioned Data Set which    "
   Say "             will be edited.                                "
   Say
   Say "       Macro is the name of a macro to execute.  If it      "
   Say "             is a program macro, remember to specify the    "
   Say "             exclamation point before the name.             "
   Say
   Say "       A question mark (?) as the first parameter will      "
   Say "       cause this built in documentation to display.        "
   Say
   Exit(1)
./       ADD   NAME=XCOPY
/**  REXX -- COPY A DATA SET OR MEMBER INTO THE EDITED FILE  **/
   NUMERIC DIGITS 20
   SAVEMSG = MSG()
   X = MSG("OFF")
   X = ADDRESS()
   SUBCOM ISPEXEC
   IF RC <> 0 THEN DO
      SAY "XCOPY MUST BE RUN UNDER ISPF EDIT!"
      EXIT(0)
      END
   SUBCOM ISREDIT
   UMODE = "ISREDIT"
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC "CONTROL ERRORS RETURN"

   ADDRESS ISREDIT
   "MACRO (INFILE FROMREC TOREC) NOPROCESS"
   UPPER INFILE
   IF INFILE = '' THEN SIGNAL DISPDOC
   DSNSTATUS = SYSDSN(INFILE)
   IF DSNSTATUS <> "OK" THEN DO
      SAY INFILE DSNSTATUS ":("
      EXIT(0)
   END
   IF FROMREC <> '' THEN DO
      IF ¬DATATYPE(FROMREC,'W') THEN DO
         SAY "FROM RECORD NUMBER, "FROMREC", NOT NUMERIC :("
         SIGNAL QUIT
      END
   END
   ELSE FROMREC = 1
   IF TOREC <> '' THEN DO
      IF ¬DATATYPE(TOREC,'W') THEN DO
         SAY "TO RECORD NUMBER, "TOREC", NOT NUMERIC :("
         SIGNAL QUIT
      END
   END
   ELSE TOREC = 999999999

   "ISREDIT PROCESS DEST"
   IF RC = 0 THEN "ISREDIT (ZDEST) = LINENUM .ZDEST"
             ELSE ZDEST = 0

   ADDRESS TSO
   "FREE DD($$INDATA)"
   "ALLOCATE DD($$INDATA) DSN("INFILE") SHR BUFNO(30)"

   ADDRESS ISREDIT
   ADDRESS TSO "EXECIO   0 DISKR" $$INDATA "(OPEN"
   ADDRESS TSO "EXECIO 200 DISKR" $$INDATA "(STEM RECS."
   RETCODE  = RC
   READREC  = 0
   INSERTED = 0
   II = ZDEST
   DO WHILE RETCODE = 0
      DO JJ = 1 TO RECS.0
         READREC = READREC + 1
         IF  READREC >= FROMREC  &  READREC <= TOREC  THEN DO
            INDATA = RECS.JJ
            "ISREDIT LINE_AFTER &II = (INDATA)"
            II = II + 1
            INSERTED = INSERTED + 1
         END
         ELSE IF READREC > TOREC THEN SIGNAL QUIT0
      END
      ADDRESS TSO "EXECIO 200 DISKR" $$INDATA "(STEM RECS."
      RETCODE = RC
   END
   IF RETCODE = 2 THEN DO
      DO JJ = 1 TO RECS.0
         READREC = READREC + 1
         IF  READREC >= FROMREC  &  READREC <= TOREC  THEN DO
            INDATA = RECS.JJ
            "ISREDIT LINE_AFTER &II = (INDATA)"
            II = II + 1
            INSERTED = INSERTED + 1
         END
         ELSE IF READREC > TOREC THEN SIGNAL QUIT0
      END
   END

QUIT0:
   ADDRESS TSO "EXECIO 0 DISKR" $$INDATA "(FINIS"
   ADDRESS TSO "FREE DD($$INDATA)"

QUIT:
   IF ZDEST = 0 THEN ZDEST = 1
                ELSE ZDEST = ZDEST + 1
   "ISREDIT CURSOR = " ZDEST 1
   CALL SETMSG '* NO ' INSERTED 'RECORDS INSERTED$RECORDS COPIED'
   RETURN

SETMSG:
   PARSE ARG ZERRHM ZERRALRM ZERRSM'$'ZERRLM
   ADDRESS ISPEXEC 'SETMSG MSG(ISRZ002) COND'
   RETURN

DISPDOC:
   ADDRESS TSO "CLEAR"
   SAY "XCOPY - COPY ANY DATASET OR MEMBER DIRECTLY INTO EDITED FILE "
   SAY
   SAY " FORMAT "
   SAY "    XCOPY  FILE-NAME ( FROM-REC# ( TO-REC# ) )               "
   SAY "       THE FILE NAME OR PDS MEMBER NAME IS MANDATORY.  IF    "
   SAY "       SPECIFIED, ONLY THE RECORDS INCLUDING THE FROM-REC#   "
   SAY "       TO THE TO-REC# (OR TO THE END OF THE FILE IF NO       "
   SAY "       TO-REC# IS SPECIFIED) WILL BE COPIED.  A DESTINATION  "
   SAY "       (EITHER AN 'A' OR 'B' IN THE PREFIX AREA) MAY BE      "
   SAY "       SPECIFIED; IF NONE IS SPECIFIED, THE DATA IS COPIED   "
   SAY "       TO THE FRONT OF THE EDITED FILE.                      "
   SAY
   SAY " EXAMPLE "
   SAY "    XCOPY  'SYS1.MACLIB(GET)' "
   SAY "       WILL COPY THE 'GET' MEMBER OF SYS1.MACLIB INTO        "
   SAY "       THE EDITIED FILE, EITHER TO THE BEGINNING OR TO       "
   SAY "       WHERE THE AFTER/BEFORE PREFIX WAS SPECIFIED.          "
   SAY
   EXIT(1)
./       ADD   NAME=ZVW
/* REXX -- ZVW  -- View the dataset the cursor is on                */

/* This edit macro allows the user to VIEW the dataset located on   */
/* the line that the cursor is on.  If the dataset name contains &  */
/* tokens, i.e.  is within a PROC, ZVW will attempt to interpolate  */
/* the proper variables if they are defaulted on the PROC. It now   */
/* opens a new screen session for the View.                         */

  Address ISREDIT
  "MACRO (parms)"
  If parms = "?" then signal DispDoc
  Address ISPEXEC "CONTROL ERRORS RETURN"
  "(row,col) = CURSOR"
  "(data1)   = LINE  " row
  dsnstart = Pos("DSN=",data1)       /* look for DSN=              */
  If dsnstart = 0 then do
    dsnstart = Pos("DSNAME=",data1)  /* look for DSNAME=           */
    If dsnstart = 0 then do
      If col < 1 then dsnstart = 1   /* look for delimiters        */
      Else do
        Do ii = col to 1 by -1
          while substr(data1,ii,1) <> " " & substr(data1,ii,1) <> "'"
        End ii
        If ii <  1 then dsnstart = 1
                   else dsnstart = ii + 1
      End
    End
    Else dsnstart = dsnstart + 7     /* DSNAME= specified in JCL   */
  End
  Else dsnstart = dsnstart + 4       /* DSN = specified in JCL     */
  dsnend = Pos(",",data1,dsnstart)   /* look for end of dsn        */
  If dsnend = 0 then do
    dsnend = Pos(" ",data1,dsnstart)
    If dsnend = 0 then do
      dsnend = Pos("'",data1,dsnstart)
      If dsnend = 0 then do
        zedsmsg = "No end of DSN"
        zedlmsg = "The data set name is not terminated with a" ,
                  "space or comma."
        Address ISPEXEC "SETMSG MSG(ISRZ001)"    /* msg - with alarm */
        "CURSOR = " row col
        Exit 8
      End
    End
  End
  dsnend = dsnend - 1
  dsn = Substr(data1,dsnstart,dsnend-dsnstart+1) /* extract dsn     */
  If pos(dsn,'&') <> 0 then call Try_If_Proc
  Address ISPEXEC "SELECT PGM(ISPSTRT)",
     "PARM(CMD(ISREPDF '"dsn"' V))"
         /*** Address ISPEXEC "VIEW DATASET('"dsn"')" ***/
  If RC <> 0 then Address ISPEXEC "SETMSG MSG("ZERRMSG")"
  "CURSOR = " row col
  Exit 0

Try_If_Proc:
  "(proc1) = LINE" 1
  If pos(proc1," PROC ") <> 0 then do
    Do ii = 71 to 1 by -1 while substr(proc1,ii,1) = " "
    End
    If substr(proc1,ii,1) = "," | substr(proc1,ii-4,5) <> " PROC",
      then call Process_Proc
  End
  Return

Process_Proc:
  Call Get_Vary
  xx = pos(dsn,"&")
  Do while xx <> 0
    Do yy = xx+1 to length(dsn),
      while substr(dsn,yy,1) <> "."
    End
    sought  = substr(dsn,xx+1,yy-xx-1)
    substit = Vary.sought
    If yy < length(dsn) then dsn = substr(dsn,1,xx-1),
      || substit || substr(dsn,yy+1)
    Else dsn = substr(dsn,1,xx-1) || substit
    xx = pos(dsn,"&")
  End
  Return

Get_Vary:
  jj = pos(proc1,"=")
  ll = 1
  do while jj <> 0
    If substr(proc1,1,3) = "//*" then do
      ll = ll + 1
      "(proc1) = LINE" ll
      jj = pos(proc1,"=")
    End
    Else do
      do mm = jj-1 to 1 by -1,
        while substr(proc1,mm,1) <> " ",
          & substr(proc1,mm,1) <> ","
      end
      stemy = substr(proc1,mm+1,jj-mm-1)
      do nn = jj+1 to 71,
        while substr(proc1,nn,1) <> " " & substr(proc1,nn,1) <> ","
      end
      hashy = substr(proc1,jj+1,nn-jj-1)
      hashy = strip(hashy,B,"'")
      Vary.stemy = hashy
      proc1 = substr(proc1,1,mm),
        || copies(" ",nn-mm+1) || substr(proc1,nn)
      jj = pos(proc1,"=")
    End
    If jj = 0 then do
      Do ii = 71 to 1 by -1 while substr(proc1,ii,1) = " "
      End
      If substr(proc1,ii,1) = "," then do
        ll = ll + 1
        "(proc1) = LINE" ll
        jj = pos(proc1,"=")
      End
      Else jj = 0
    End
  End
  Return

DispDoc:
  ADDRESS TSO "CLEAR"
  Say "ZVW  --  View dataset under cursor                          "
  Say
  Say "   ZVW  ( ? )                                               "
  Say
  Say "       This macro will attempt to View the dataset on which "
  Say "       the cursor is positioned. If the dataset contains    "
  Say "       PROC substitutions such as &XX, the macro will try   "
  Say "       to fill in the variables from any PROC statement at  "
  Say "       the top of the file.                                 "
  Say
  Say "       A question mark (?) as the first parameter will      "
  Say "       cause this built in documentation to display.        "
  Say
  Exit(1)


